### [51] [Attention-Gated Convolutional Networks for Scanner-Agnostic Quality Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15059)
*Chinmay Bakhale,Anil Sao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种混合CNN-注意力框架，用于鲁棒、站点无关的MRI质量评估。该模型结合2D CNN编码器提取局部空间特征与多头交叉注意力机制建模全局依赖，有效识别运动伪影（如振铃、模糊），同时过滤站点特异性强度变化和背景噪声。在MR-ART数据集上训练，并在已见站点和未见站点（ABIDE）上评估。在已见站点上达到0.9920的准确率和0.9919的F1分数；在未见站点上仍保持0.755的准确率，无需微调，表明其对域偏移具有强鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 运动伪影严重影响结构MRI的质量，传统手动质量控制难以应对大规模纵向研究的可扩展性挑战。需要一种自动、通用且跨站点稳定的MRI质量评估方法。

Method: 采用层次化2D CNN编码器提取局部空间特征，结合多头交叉注意力机制捕捉全局依赖关系，实现对运动相关伪影的优先关注和对站点特异性干扰的动态抑制。模型在MR-ART数据集上端到端训练，使用200名受试者平衡样本。

Conclusion: 基于注意力的特征重加权能有效捕获普遍存在的伪影特征，显著缩小不同成像环境与扫描仪之间的性能差距，为大规模自动化MRI质量评估提供了可靠解决方案。

Abstract: Motion artifacts present a significant challenge in structural MRI (sMRI), often compromising clinical diagnostics and large-scale automated analysis. While manual quality control (QC) remains the gold standard, it is increasingly unscalable for massive longitudinal studies. To address this, we propose a hybrid CNN-Attention framework designed for robust, site-invariant MRI quality assessment. Our architecture integrates a hierarchical 2D CNN encoder for local spatial feature extraction with a multi-head cross-attention mechanism to model global dependencies. This synergy enables the model to prioritize motion relevant artifact signatures, such as ringing and blurring, while dynamically filtering out site-specific intensity variations and background noise. The framework was trained end-to-end on the MR-ART dataset using a balanced cohort of 200 subjects. Performance was evaluated across two tiers: Seen Site Evaluation on a held-out MR-ART partition and Unseen Site Evaluation using 200 subjects from 17 heterogeneous sites in the ABIDE archive. On seen sites, the model achieved a scan-level accuracy of 0.9920 and an F1-score of 0.9919. Crucially, it maintained strong generalization across unseen ABIDE sites (Acc = 0.755) without any retraining or fine-tuning, demonstrating high resilience to domain shift. These results indicate that attention-based feature re-weighting successfully captures universal artifact descriptors, bridging the performance gap between diverse imaging environments and scanner manufacturers.

### [52] [Learning Where to Embed: Noise-Aware Positional Embedding for Query Retrieval in Small-Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15065)
*Yangchen Zeng,Zhenyu Yu,Dongming Jiang,Wenbo Zhang,Yifan Hong,Zhanhua Hu,Jiao Luo,Kangning Cui*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出HELP框架，通过热图引导的位置-语义融合机制，有效抑制背景噪声，提升小目标检测效率与准确性。核心是热图引导的位置嵌入（HPE），在编码器和解码器中分别实现噪声抑制与高质量查询检索，结合线性蛇形卷积增强特征表达，仅在训练阶段使用梯度热图监督，推理无额外开销。模型减少解码层数至3层，参数量降低59.4%（66.3M vs. 163M），在多个基准上保持高精度并降低计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer-based检测器在小目标检测中虽有进展，但存在效率低、易受背景噪声干扰的问题，尤其在查询质量差时影响性能，因此需要更高效的解码机制来优化低质量查询。

Method: 提出HELP框架，采用热图引导的位置嵌入（HPE）机制，在编码器中注入热图感知的位置编码以抑制背景噪声，在解码器中通过基于梯度的掩码过滤掉主导背景的嵌入，同时引入线性蛇形卷积增强复杂小目标的特征表示；训练阶段使用梯度热图监督，推理无额外开销。

Result: 解码层数从8层降至3层，参数量减少59.4%（66.3M vs. 163M），在多个基准测试中保持一致的精度提升，且在更低计算预算下表现优异。

Conclusion: HELP框架通过位置-语义融合与噪声感知设计，显著提升了小目标检测的效率与鲁棒性，为轻量化高效检测提供了新范式。

Abstract: Transformer-based detectors have advanced small-object detection, but they often remain inefficient and vulnerable to background-induced query noise, which motivates deep decoders to refine low-quality queries. We present HELP (Heatmap-guided Embedding Learning Paradigm), a noise-aware positional-semantic fusion framework that studies where to embed positional information by selectively preserving positional encodings in foreground-salient regions while suppressing background clutter. Within HELP, we introduce Heatmap-guided Positional Embedding (HPE) as the core embedding mechanism and visualize it with a heatbar for interpretable diagnosis and fine-tuning. HPE is integrated into both the encoder and decoder: it guides noise-suppressed feature encoding by injecting heatmap-aware positional encoding, and it enables high-quality query retrieval by filtering background-dominant embeddings via a gradient-based mask filter before decoding. To address feature sparsity in complex small targets, we integrate Linear-Snake Convolution to enrich retrieval-relevant representations. The gradient-based heatmap supervision is used during training only, incurring no additional gradient computation at inference. As a result, our design reduces decoder layers from eight to three and achieves a 59.4% parameter reduction (66.3M vs. 163M) while maintaining consistent accuracy gains under a reduced compute budget across benchmarks. Code Repository: https://github.com/yidimopozhibai/Noise-Suppressed-Query-Retrieval

### [53] [Building Extraction from Remote Sensing Imagery under Hazy and Low-light Conditions: Benchmark and Baseline](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15088)
*Feifei Sang,Wei Lu,Hongruixuan Chen,Sibao Chen,Bin Luo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出首个针对雾霾和低光条件下建筑物提取的光学遥感基准数据集HaLoBuilding，结合多时相配对策略确保标签精度。基于此，提出HaLoBuild-Net框架，通过空间-频率聚焦模块（SFFM）、全局多尺度引导模块（GMGM）和互导融合模块（MGFM），有效应对气象干扰与几何模糊问题，在多个数据集上表现优异且具备良好泛化能力。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用同场景多时相配对策略构建高保真标注数据集HaLoBuilding；提出HaLoBuild-Net端到端框架，包含：空间-频率聚焦模块（SFFM）用于联合大感受野注意力与频域感知通道重加权，利用稳定低频特征抑制气象干扰；全局多尺度引导模块（GMGM）提供语义约束以保持建筑拓扑结构；互导融合模块（MGFM）实现双向语义-空间校准，抑制浅层噪声并锐化模糊边界。

Abstract: Building extraction from optical Remote Sensing (RS) imagery suffers from performance degradation under real-world hazy and low-light conditions. However, existing optical methods and benchmarks focus primarily on ideal clear-weather conditions. While SAR offers all-weather sensing, its side-looking geometry causes geometric distortions. To address these challenges, we introduce HaLoBuilding, the first optical benchmark specifically designed for building extraction under hazy and low-light conditions. By leveraging a same-scene multitemporal pairing strategy, we ensure pixel-level label alignment and high fidelity even under extreme degradation. Building upon this benchmark, we propose HaLoBuild-Net, a novel end-to-end framework for building extraction in adverse RS scenarios. At its core, we develop a Spatial-Frequency Focus Module (SFFM) to effectively mitigate meteorological interference on building features by coupling large receptive field attention with frequency-aware channel reweighting guided by stable low-frequency anchors. Additionally, a Global Multi-scale Guidance Module (GMGM) provides global semantic constraints to anchor building topologies, while a Mutual-Guided Fusion Module (MGFM) implements bidirectional semantic-spatial calibration to suppress shallow noise and sharpen weather-induced blurred boundaries. Extensive experiments demonstrate that HaLoBuild-Net significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods and conventional cascaded restoration-segmentation paradigms on the HaLoBuilding dataset, while maintaining robust generalization on WHU, INRIA, and LoveDA datasets. The source code and datasets are publicly available at: https://github.com/AeroVILab-AHU/HaLoBuilding.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖纯视觉特征，在光照变化或衣物改变时性能显著下降，缺乏对身份不变特征的有效建模。

Method: 使用指令引导大视觉语言模型生成身份内在的语义文本；基于该文本进行语义驱动的视觉标记过滤（SVTF）以增强关键视觉区域；同时通过语义驱动的专家路由（SER）实现多场景鲁棒的门控机制。

Result: 在AT-USTC数据集上达到领先性能，并在5个主流ReID基准上展现优异泛化能力，表现极具竞争力。

Conclusion: 所提STFER框架有效融合语义先验与视觉特征，显著提升了行人重识别在复杂条件下的鲁棒性与泛化能力。

Abstract: Any-Time Person Re-identification (AT-ReID) necessitates the robust retrieval of target individuals under arbitrary conditions, encompassing both modality shifts (daytime and nighttime) and extensive clothing-change scenarios, ranging from short-term to long-term intervals. However, existing methods are highly relying on pure visual features, which are prone to change due to environmental and time factors, resulting in significantly performance deterioration under scenarios involving illumination caused modality shifts or cloth-change. In this paper, we propose Semantic-driven Token Filtering and Expert Routing (STFER), a novel framework that leverages the ability of Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) to generate identity consistency text, which provides identity-discriminative features that are robust to both clothing variations and cross-modality shifts between RGB and IR. Specifically, we employ instructions to guide the LVLM in generating identity-intrinsic semantic text that captures biometric constants for the semantic model driven. The text token is further used for Semantic-driven Visual Token Filtering (SVTF), which enhances informative visual regions and suppresses redundant background noise. Meanwhile, the text token is also used for Semantic-driven Expert Routing (SER), which integrates the semantic text into expert routing, resulting in more robust multi-scenario gating. Extensive experiments on the Any-Time ReID dataset (AT-USTC) demonstrate that our model achieves state-of-the-art results. Moreover, the model trained on AT-USTC was evaluated across 5 widely-used ReID benchmarks demonstrating superior generalization capabilities with highly competitive results. Our code will be available soon.

Existing masked autoencoder (MAE) approaches typically process images or short clips independently, failing to capture the inherent multi-view structure required for coherent cardiac representation. This allows the model to aggregate variable-length sequences and distinct views, reconstructing a holistic representation of cardiac function from partial observations. *Olga Loginova,Frank Keller*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出PIE-V框架，通过心理学启发的误差注入生成真实可信的错误与纠正视频，结合LLM进行文本重写与验证，实现对自指性程序视频中错误和恢复行为的可控生成与评估。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有程序性数据集在人类错误及后续纠正方面覆盖不足，且错误与修正痕迹不一致；在第一人称视角视频中，错误常被手部遮挡，仅通过微小物体状态变化体现，难以捕捉。因此需要一种可控制、符合人类行为模式的误差注入方法来增强数据多样性与真实性。

Method: PIE-V框架包括：基于任务阶段和语义步骤负荷的心理学启发误差规划器、建模恢复行为的纠错规划器、执行级联一致重写的LLM写作者，以及验证流程连贯性和修复失败的LLM评判器；视频片段编辑采用文本引导的视频生成技术合成替换片段，并无缝拼接至原视频以保持视觉合理性。

Abstract: Reliable procedural monitoring in video requires exposure to naturally occurring human errors and the recoveries that follow. In egocentric recordings, mistakes are often partially occluded by hands and revealed through subtle object state changes, while existing procedural datasets provide limited and inconsistent mistake and correction traces. We present PIE-V (Psychologically Inspired Error injection for Videos), a framework for constructing and benchmarking mistake-aware egocentric procedural videos by augmenting clean keystep procedures with controlled, human-plausible deviations. PIE-V combines a psychology-informed error planner conditioned on procedure phase and semantic step load, a correction planner that models recovery behavior, an LLM writer that performs cascade-consistent rewrites, and an LLM judge that validates procedural coherence and repairs failures. For video segment edits, PIE-V synthesizes replacement clips with text-guided video generation and stitches them into the episode to preserve visual plausibility. Applied to 17 tasks and 50 Ego-Exo4D scenarios, PIE-V injects 102 mistakes and generates 27 recovery corrections. For benchmarking, we introduce a unified taxonomy and a human rubric with nine metrics that cover step-level and procedure-level quality, including plausibility, procedure logic with annotator confidence, state change coherence, and grounding between text and video. Using this protocol, we audit several existing resources and compare PIE-V against a freeform LLM generation baseline under the same criteria. Together, the framework and rubric support post-completion verification for egocentric procedural mistake detection and correction.

### [57] [Class Unlearning via Depth-Aware Removal of Forget-Specific Directions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15166)
*Arman Hatami,Romina Aalishah,Ilya E. Monosov*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DAMP是一种无需梯度优化的一次性权重手术方法，用于从预训练模型中移除特定类别的知识。它通过在每一层计算类别原型，提取与保留类别相比的遗忘方向，并使用投影更新减少对这些方向的敏感性。为保持模型性能，DAMP采用基于探测可分性的无参数深度感知缩放规则，在浅层进行较小修改，深层进行较大修改。该方法可扩展至多类遗忘，通过低秩子空间移除实现。在多个数据集和架构上，DAMP比现有方法更接近重训练基准，表现出更强的选择性遗忘、更好的保留类别性能以及更少的深层残留遗忘结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有类遗忘方法常表现出弱或负选择性，未能真正移除遗忘类的信息，其表象遗忘可能源于分类器头部抑制而非表示层面的删除。此外，许多方法依赖最终层偏置调整，缺乏对内部表示的实质性清理。因此需要一种能有效清除遗忘类结构且不影响保留类性能的方法。

Method: DAMP（Depth-Aware Modulation by Projection）通过计算下一层可学习模块输入空间中的类别原型，将遗忘类方向作为相对于保留类原型的残差提取，并应用投影方式更新权重以降低对这些方向的敏感性。同时引入深度感知缩放规则，根据探针可分性动态调节各层修改强度，确保早期层改动小、深层改动大。支持多类遗忘的低秩子空间移除机制。

Result: 在MNIST、CIFAR-10、CIFAR-100和Tiny ImageNet上，DAMP在多种卷积和Transformer架构中均表现优于已有方法，更接近重训练标准；实现了更强的选择性遗忘，保留了更高的保留类准确率，显著减少了深层表示中残留的遗忘类结构。

Conclusion: DAMP提供了一种高效、闭式、无需重新训练的类遗忘方案，能够真正移除遗忘类信息，同时最小化对保留类性能的影响，是目前最接近重训练效果的单次权重修改方法之一。

Abstract: Machine unlearning aims to remove targeted knowledge from a trained model without the cost of retraining from scratch. In class unlearning, however, reducing accuracy on forget classes does not necessarily imply true forgetting: forgotten information can remain encoded in internal representations, and apparent forgetting may arise from classifier-head suppression rather than representational removal. We show that existing class-unlearning methods often exhibit weak or negative selectivity, preserve forget-class structure in deep representations, or rely heavily on final-layer bias shifts. We then introduce DAMP (Depth-Aware Modulation by Projection), a one-shot, closed-form weight-surgery method that removes forget-specific directions from a pretrained network without gradient-based optimization. At each stage, DAMP computes class prototypes in the input space of the next learnable operator, extracts forget directions as residuals relative to retain-class prototypes, and applies a projection-based update to reduce downstream sensitivity to those directions. To preserve utility, DAMP uses a parameter-free depth-aware scaling rule derived from probe separability, applying smaller edits in early layers and larger edits in deeper layers. The method naturally extends to multi-class forgetting through low-rank subspace removal. Across MNIST, CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, and Tiny ImageNet, and across convolutional and transformer architectures, DAMP more closely resembles the retraining gold standard than some of the prior methods, improving selective forgetting while better preserving retain-class performance and reducing residual forget-class structure in deep layers.

</details>

Abstract: Adverse lighting conditions, such as cast shadows and irregular illumination, pose significant challenges to computer vision systems by degrading visibility and color fidelity. ### [59] [Boundary-Centric Active Learning for Temporal Action Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15173)
*Halil Ismail Helvaci,Sen-ching Samson Cheung*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: B-ACT是一种针对时间动作分割（TAS）的剪辑预算内主动学习框架，通过聚焦高影响力的动作边界区域来提升标注效率。它采用两级循环机制：首先基于预测不确定性对未标注视频进行排序与查询；其次在选定视频中，利用融合邻域不确定性、类别模糊性和时间预测动态的新型边界得分，识别并选择前K个候选边界。该方法仅要求标注边界帧，但通过以边界为中心的剪辑训练，充分利用模型感受野中的时序上下文信息。在GTEA、50Salads和Breakfast数据集上的实验表明，这种边界中心的监督策略在稀疏标注预算下显著优于现有主动学习基线和先进方法，尤其在边界定位主导评估指标的数据集上表现突出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间动作分割（TAS）需要密集的时间标注，而大部分标注成本集中在动作转换区域，这些区域是分割错误的主要来源，且微小的时间偏移会显著降低评估分数。因此，需要一种更高效的标注策略，将有限的标注资源集中于最具信息量的边界区域，以提升标注效率和模型性能。

Method: B-ACT采用两阶段主动学习框架：(i) 基于预测不确定性对未标注视频进行排序并选择最有价值的样本；(ii) 在每个选中的视频中，从当前模型预测中提取候选动作边界，并使用一种结合邻域不确定性、类别模糊性和时间预测动态的边界得分函数，选出前K个最值得标注的边界。标注仅限于边界帧，但训练时使用围绕边界的时间片段，以保留时序上下文信息。

Result: 在GTEA、50Salads和Breakfast数据集上，B-ACT在稀疏标注预算下表现出卓越的标签效率，持续超越现有的主动学习基线和最先进的方法。在边界定位对评估结果影响较大的数据集上，其性能提升最为显著。

Conclusion: B-ACT通过聚焦动作边界区域的主动学习策略，实现了高效且精准的时间动作分割，在有限标注资源下显著提升了模型性能，尤其适用于依赖精确边界定位的任务场景。

Abstract: Temporal action segmentation (TAS) demands dense temporal supervision, yet most of the annotation cost in untrimmed videos is spent identifying and refining action transitions, where segmentation errors concentrate and small temporal shifts disproportionately degrade segmental metrics. We introduce B-ACT, a clip-budgeted active learning framework that explicitly allocates supervision to these high-leverage boundary regions. B-ACT operates in a hierarchical two-stage loop: (i) it ranks and queries unlabeled videos using predictive uncertainty, and (ii) within each selected video, it detects candidate transitions from the current model predictions and selects the top-$K$ boundaries via a novel boundary score that fuses neighborhood uncertainty, class ambiguity, and temporal predictive dynamics. Importantly, our annotation protocol requests labels for only the boundary frames while still training on boundary-centered clips to exploit temporal context through the model's receptive field. Extensive experiments on GTEA, 50Salads, and Breakfast demonstrate that boundary-centric supervision delivers strong label efficiency and consistently surpasses representative TAS active learning baselines and prior state of the art under sparse budgets, with the largest gains on datasets where boundary placement dominates edit and overlap-based F1 scores.

### [60] [VisPCO: Visual Token Pruning Configuration Optimization via Budget-Aware Pareto-Frontier Learning for Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15188)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Visual token pruning methods effectively mitigate the quadratic computational growth caused by processing high-resolution images and video frames in vision-language models (VLMs). However, existing approaches rely on predefined pruning configurations without determining whether they achieve computation-performance optimality. In this work, we introduce , a novel framework that formulates visual token pruning as a Pareto configuration optimization problem to automatically identify optimal configurations. Our approach employs continuous relaxation and straight-through estimators to enable gradient-based search, solved via the Augmented Lagrangian method. Extensive experiments across 8 visual benchmarks demonstrate that effectively approximates the empirical Pareto frontier obtained through grid search and generalizes well across various pruning methods and VLM architectures. Furthermore, through learnable kernel functions, we investigate layer-wise pruning patterns and reveal that multi-step progressive pruning captures VLMs' hierarchical compression structure, achieving superior accuracy-efficiency trade-offs compared to single-layer approaches.

### [61] [Unsupervised Skeleton-Based Action Segmentation via Hierarchical Spatiotemporal Vector Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15196)

TL;DR: 提出一种新型分层时空向量量化框架，用于无监督骨架动作分割。通过两级向量量化，低层关联细粒度子动作，高层聚合子动作为动作级表示；进一步结合时空信息，实现多层级聚类与输入骨架及时间戳的恢复。在HuGaDB、LARa、BABEL等多个基准上表现优异，达到新最佳性能并减少片段长度偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在无监督骨架动作分割中难以有效捕捉细粒度子动作与动作级语义之间的层次关系，且常忽略时间信息，导致分割结果存在长度偏差。因此需要一种能同时利用空间和时间信息的分层结构来提升性能。

Method: 提出分层时空向量量化框架：首先设计双层向量量化机制，低层对骨架进行细粒度子动作编码，高层聚合子动作形成动作级表征；随后引入时间维度，联合优化空间重建与时间对齐，实现多层级聚类与骨架及时间戳的同步恢复。

Result: 在多个公开数据集（HuGaDB、LARa、BABEL）上显著优于现有方法，达到新的状态领先水平，同时有效缓解了传统方法中存在的段落长度偏差问题。

Conclusion: 所提出的分层时空向量量化框架能够有效建模骨架动作的层次结构，并融合时空信息，在无监督条件下实现更准确、鲁棒的动作分割，为未来研究提供了新思路。

Specifically, the lower level associates skeletons with fine-grained subactions, while the higher level further aggregates subactions into action-level representations. Our hierarchical approach outperforms the non-hierarchical baseline, while primarily exploiting spatial cues by reconstructing input skeletons. Next, we extend our approach by leveraging both spatial and temporal information, yielding a hierarchical spatiotemporal vector quantization scheme. In particular, our hierarchical spatiotemporal approach performs multi-level clustering, while simultaneously recovering input skeletons and their corresponding timestamps. Lastly, extensive experiments on multiple benchmarks, including HuGaDB, LARa, and BABEL, demonstrate that our approach establishes a new state-of-the-art performance and reduces segment length bias in unsupervised skeleton-based temporal action segmentation.

</details>


### [62] [StreamCacheVGGT: Streaming Visual Geometry Transformers with Robust Scoring and Hybrid Cache Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15237)
*Xuanyi Liu,Deyi Ji,Chunan Yu,Qi Zhu,Xuanfu Li,Jin Ma,Tianrun Chen,Lanyun Zhu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: StreamCacheVGGT 是一种无需训练的框架，通过 Cross-Layer Consistency-Enhanced Scoring (CLCES) 和 Hybrid Cache Compression (HCC) 两个模块，解决传统 $O(1)$ 框架中因二进制删除和局部评分导致的信息丢失与评估噪声问题。CLCES 利用跨层轨迹分析识别持续的几何显著性，减少激活噪声；HCC 采用三阶段筛选策略，将中等重要性的令牌合并到保留锚点中，从而在保持常量内存预算的同时，显著提升三维重建精度与长期稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 $O(1)$ 框架依赖纯淘汰机制，造成信息破坏和评估噪声，影响连续视频流中的 3D 重建稳定性与准确性。

Method: 提出 StreamCacheVGGT 框架，包含 CLCES 模块（基于跨层一致性分析的评分机制）和 HCC 模块（三层次混合压缩策略，通过键向量流形上的最近邻分配实现令牌融合），实现高效且稳定的缓存管理。

Conclusion: StreamCacheVGGT 通过创新的缓存管理机制，在不增加计算负担的前提下，有效缓解了信息丢失与评分噪声问题，为连续视频流下的高保真 3D 重建提供了可靠解决方案。

Abstract: Reconstructing dense 3D geometry from continuous video streams requires stable inference under a constant memory budget. Existing $O(1)$ frameworks primarily rely on a ``pure eviction'' paradigm, which suffers from significant information destruction due to binary token deletion and evaluation noise from localized, single-layer scoring. To address these bottlenecks, we propose StreamCacheVGGT, a training-free framework that reimagines cache management through two synergistic modules: Cross-Layer Consistency-Enhanced Scoring (CLCES) and Hybrid Cache Compression (HCC). CLCES mitigates activation noise by tracking token importance trajectories across the Transformer hierarchy, employing order-statistical analysis to identify sustained geometric salience. Leveraging these robust scores, HCC transcends simple eviction by introducing a three-tier triage strategy that merges moderately important tokens into retained anchors via nearest-neighbor assignment on the key-vector manifold. This approach preserves essential geometric context that would otherwise be lost. Extensive evaluations on five benchmarks (7-Scenes, NRGBD, ETH3D, Bonn, and KITTI) demonstrate that StreamCacheVGGT sets a new state-of-the-art, delivering superior reconstruction accuracy and long-term stability while strictly adhering to constant-cost constraints.

### [63] [TokenGS: Decoupling 3D Gaussian Prediction from Pixels with Learnable Tokens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15239)
*Jiawei Ren,Michal Jan Tyszkiewicz,Jiahui Huang,Zan Gojcic*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了现代基于Transformer的前馈3D高斯溅射（3DGS）预测方法中的若干关键设计选择，提出直接回归3D均值坐标而非沿相机射线回归深度，采用自监督渲染损失，使模型从编码器-only架构转变为可学习高斯标记的编码器-解码器架构。该方法实现了与输入图像分辨率和视角数量解耦的预测原语数，提升了对姿态噪声和多视图不一致性的鲁棒性，并支持高效的测试时优化，同时保持学习到的先验知识。TokenGS在静态与动态场景中均达到最先进的前馈重建性能，生成更规则的几何结构和更均衡的3DGS分布，并能自然恢复静态-动态分解和场景流等新兴属性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法中将高斯均值作为沿相机射线的深度进行回归存在次优性，且限制了模型灵活性与泛化能力，尤其在面对姿态噪声或多视图不一致时表现不佳。因此需要一种更直接、更灵活的建模方式以提升性能与鲁棒性。

Method: 提出直接回归3D均值坐标，使用自监督渲染损失训练；引入编码器-解码器架构与可学习的高斯标记，实现预测原语数与输入分辨率及视角数解耦。通过标记空间的测试时优化增强模型适应性。

Result: TokenGS在静态与动态场景下均取得当前最优的前馈重建性能，几何结构更规则，3DGS分布更均衡，具备自然恢复静态-动态分解和场景流的能力，对姿态噪声和多视图不一致具有更强鲁棒性，且支持高效测试时优化而不破坏已有先验。

Conclusion: 通过重构3DGS预测的建模范式，提出的TokenGS方法显著提升了前馈3D高斯溅射的性能与鲁棒性，为后续研究提供了新的设计思路。

Abstract: In this work, we revisit several key design choices of modern Transformer-based approaches for feed-forward 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) prediction. We argue that the common practice of regressing Gaussian means as depths along camera rays is suboptimal, and instead propose to directly regress 3D mean coordinates using only a self-supervised rendering loss. This formulation allows us to move from the standard encoder-only design to an encoder-decoder architecture with learnable Gaussian tokens, thereby unbinding the number of predicted primitives from input image resolution and number of views. Our resulting method, TokenGS, demonstrates improved robustness to pose noise and multiview inconsistencies, while naturally supporting efficient test-time optimization in token space without degrading learned priors. TokenGS achieves state-of-the-art feed-forward reconstruction performance on both static and dynamic scenes, producing more regularized geometry and more balanced 3DGS distribution, while seamlessly recovering emergent scene attributes such as static-dynamic decomposition and scene flow.

### [64] [Why Do Vision Language Models Struggle To Recognize Human Emotions?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15280)
*Madhav Agarwal,Sotirios A. Tsaftaris,Laura Sevilla-Lara,Steven McDonagh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文探讨了视觉语言模型（VLMs）在识别人类情绪时表现不佳的原因，指出其在处理长尾分布的情绪数据和动态时间信息方面存在两大缺陷。针对这些问题，作者提出改进采样策略以缓解类别偏差，并设计了一种多阶段上下文增强方法，通过将帧间信息转化为自然语言摘要来补充视觉输入，从而提升情绪识别性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种多阶段上下文增强策略：将密集帧序列中的“中间帧”转换为自然语言摘要，再与稀疏关键帧一同输入给VLM，以保留情感变化轨迹并避免注意力分散。同时采用替代采样策略减轻长尾分布带来的类别偏差。

Conclusion: VLMs在情绪识别上的失败源于其对长尾数据分布的敏感性和对时间序列信息建模能力的不足。通过引入上下文增强和优化采样策略，可有效改善其性能，为未来智能系统的情感理解提供新方向。

Abstract: Understanding emotions is a fundamental ability for intelligent systems to be able to interact with humans. Vision-language models (VLMs) have made tremendous progress in the last few years for many visual tasks, potentially offering a promising solution for understanding emotions. However, it is surprising that even the most sophisticated contemporary VLMs struggle to recognize human emotions or to outperform even specialized vision-only classifiers. In this paper we ask the question "Why do VLMs struggle to recognize human emotions?", and observe that the inherently continuous and dynamic task of facial expression recognition (DFER) exposes two critical VLM vulnerabilities. First, emotion datasets are naturally long-tailed, and the web-scale data used to pre-train VLMs exacerbates this head-class bias, causing them to systematically collapse rare, under-represented emotions into common categories. We propose alternative sampling strategies that prevent favoring common concepts. Second, temporal information is critical for understanding emotions. However, VLMs are unable to represent temporal information over dense frame sequences, as they are limited by context size and the number of tokens that can fit in memory, which poses a clear challenge for emotion recognition. We demonstrate that the sparse temporal sampling strategy used in VLMs is inherently misaligned with the fleeting nature of micro-expressions (0.25-0.5 seconds), which are often the most critical affective signal. As a diagnostic probe, we propose a multi-stage context enrichment strategy that utilizes the information from "in-between" frames by first converting them into natural language summaries. This enriched textual context is provided as input to the VLM alongside sparse keyframes, preventing attentional dilution from excessive visual data while preserving the emotional trajectory.

### [66] [GlobalSplat: Efficient Feed-Forward 3D Gaussian Splatting via Global Scene Tokens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15284)
*Roni Itkin,Noam Issachar,Yehonatan Keypur,Yehonatan Keypur,Anpei Chen,Sagie Benaim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: GlobalSplat提出一种新的3D高斯点云拼贴框架，通过‘先对齐后解码’的策略，学习紧凑且全局一致的隐式场景表示，避免传统方法中因局部启发式分配导致的冗余与不一致性。该方法无需依赖预训练像素预测模型或密集基线的潜在特征，采用从粗到细的训练流程防止表示膨胀。在RealEstate10K和ACID数据集上，仅用16K个高斯点即实现竞争性新视角合成效果，模型体积小至4MB，推理速度低于78毫秒，显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D高斯拼贴方法在表示紧凑性、重建速度和渲染保真度之间存在显著权衡，主要由于依赖缺乏全局场景感知的局部启发式分配策略。基于前馈的方法多为像素或体素对齐，导致视图间冗余积累，随着输入视图增加，表示规模膨胀且全局一致性下降。

Method: 提出GlobalSplat框架，遵循‘对齐先于解码’原则，学习一个紧凑的全局隐式场景表示，编码多视角输入并解决跨视角对应关系，再进行显式3D几何解码。采用粗到细的训练课程逐步提升解码能力，天然抑制表示膨胀。

Result: 在RealEstate10K和ACID数据集上，仅使用16,000个高斯点即可达到与密集方法相当的新视角合成性能，模型大小仅为4MB，单次前向传播推理时间低于78毫秒，显著优于现有基线方法。

Conclusion: GlobalSplat通过全局对齐与渐进解码机制，实现了高效、紧凑且一致的3D场景重建，在保持高质量渲染的同时大幅降低存储与计算开销，为轻量化3D内容生成提供了新范式。

Abstract: The efficient spatial allocation of primitives serves as the foundation of 3D Gaussian Splatting, as it directly dictates the synergy between representation compactness, reconstruction speed, and rendering fidelity. Previous solutions, whether based on iterative optimization or feed-forward inference, suffer from significant trade-offs between these goals, mainly due to the reliance on local, heuristic-driven allocation strategies that lack global scene awareness. Specifically, current feed-forward methods are largely pixel-aligned or voxel-aligned. By unprojecting pixels into dense, view-aligned primitives, they bake redundancy into the 3D asset. As more input views are added, the representation size increases and global consistency becomes fragile. To this end, we introduce GlobalSplat, a framework built on the principle of align first, decode later. Our approach learns a compact, global, latent scene representation that encodes multi-view input and resolves cross-view correspondences before decoding any explicit 3D geometry. Crucially, this formulation enables compact, globally consistent reconstructions without relying on pretrained pixel-prediction backbones or reusing latent features from dense baselines. Utilizing a coarse-to-fine training curriculum that gradually increases decoded capacity, GlobalSplat natively prevents representation bloat. On RealEstate10K and ACID, our model achieves competitive novel-view synthesis performance while utilizing as few as 16K Gaussians, significantly less than required by dense pipelines, obtaining a light 4MB footprint. Further, GlobalSplat enables significantly faster inference than the baselines, operating under 78 milliseconds in a single forward pass. Project page is available at https://r-itk.github.io/globalsplat/

Moreover, they also rely on fixed prompt sets and rigid pipelines, offering limited flexibility for open-domain content and custom evaluation needs. To address this gap, we introduce AnimationBench, the first systematic benchmark for evaluating animation image-to-video generation. AnimationBench operationalizes the Twelve Basic Principles of Animation and IP Preservation into measurable evaluation dimensions, together with Broader Quality Dimensions including semantic consistency, motion rationality, and camera motion consistency. The benchmark supports both a standardized close-set evaluation for reproducible comparison and a flexible open-set evaluation for diagnostic analysis, and leverages visual-language models for scalable assessment. That assumption breaks down because signers often create meaning on the fly using context, space, and movement. We revisit SLT and argue that it is mainly a cross-modal reasoning task, not just a straightforward video-to-text conversion. We thus introduce a reasoning-driven SLT framework that uses an ordered sequence of latent thoughts as an explicit middle layer between the video and the generated text. These latent thoughts gradually extract and organize meaning over time. On top of this, we use a plan-then-ground decoding method: the model first decides what it wants to say, and then looks back at the video to find the evidence. This separation improves coherence and faithfulness. We also built and released a new large-scale gloss-free SLT dataset with stronger context dependencies and more realistic meanings.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于扩散的规划器虽能有效建模复杂轨迹分布，但在闭环交互中易受随机不稳定性影响，且纯模仿学习训练缺乏纠正性负反馈，导致性能受限。需提升规划器对多模态未来不确定性的建模能力，同时增强在闭环交互中的鲁棒性与优化稳定性。

Method: 提出 RAD-2 框架，包含：1）扩散生成器生成多样轨迹；2）强化学习优化的判别器重排序轨迹以评估长期驾驶质量；3）引入时序一致的组相对策略优化（TC-GRPO）缓解信用分配问题；4）设计在线生成器优化机制，将闭环反馈转化为结构化纵向信号；5）开发 BEV-Warp 仿真环境，通过空间扭曲实现在鸟瞰图特征空间的高效闭环评估。

Result: RAD-2 在模拟和真实场景中均显著提升性能：相比强基线扩散规划器，碰撞率降低 56%；真实世界部署显示感知安全性与驾驶平顺性明显改善。

Conclusion: RAD-2 通过解耦生成与判别、引入高效的强化学习优化机制与专用仿真环境，在保持轨迹多样性的同时显著提升规划稳定性与长期驾驶质量，为高阶自动驾驶提供了可扩展、鲁棒的闭环规划解决方案。

Abstract: High-level autonomous driving requires motion planners capable of modeling multimodal future uncertainties while remaining robust in closed-loop interactions. Although diffusion-based planners are effective at modeling complex trajectory distributions, they often suffer from stochastic instabilities and the lack of corrective negative feedback when trained purely with imitation learning. To address these issues, we propose RAD-2, a unified generator-discriminator framework for closed-loop planning. Specifically, a diffusion-based generator is used to produce diverse trajectory candidates, while an RL-optimized discriminator reranks these candidates according to their long-term driving quality. This decoupled design avoids directly applying sparse scalar rewards to the full high-dimensional trajectory space, thereby improving optimization stability. To further enhance reinforcement learning, we introduce Temporally Consistent Group Relative Policy Optimization, which exploits temporal coherence to alleviate the credit assignment problem. In addition, we propose On-policy Generator Optimization, which converts closed-loop feedback into structured longitudinal optimization signals and progressively shifts the generator toward high-reward trajectory manifolds. To support efficient large-scale training, we introduce BEV-Warp, a high-throughput simulation environment that performs closed-loop evaluation directly in Bird's-Eye View feature space via spatial warping. RAD-2 reduces the collision rate by 56% compared with strong diffusion-based planners. Real-world deployment further demonstrates improved perceived safety and driving smoothness in complex urban traffic.

</details>


### [70] [TokenLight: Precise Lighting Control in Images using Attribute Tokens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15310)
*Sumit Chaturvedi,Yannick Hold-Geoffroy,Mengwei Ren,Jingyuan Liu,He Zhang,Yiqun Mei,Julie Dorsey,Zhixin Shu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种图像重光照方法，通过属性令牌对光照强度、颜色、环境光、漫反射水平和3D光源位置等多维照明属性进行精确连续控制。将重光照建模为条件图像生成任务，并在大规模合成数据集上训练，结合少量真实图像提升真实感与泛化能力。实验表明，该方法在合成与真实图像上均取得领先性能，无需逆向渲染监督即可自然理解光照与几何、遮挡及材质的交互关系，在复杂场景如物体内部布光或透明材质重光照中表现优异。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有重光照方法难以实现对多种光照属性的精细、连续控制，且在复杂场景下（如物体内部布光、透明材质）效果不佳；同时缺乏对光照物理规律的隐式理解，导致结果不自然。本文旨在构建一个能精确调控多维光照属性并具备物理合理性理解能力的通用重光照框架。

Result: 在多种重光照任务中（包括场景内灯具控制、虚拟光源编辑）均达到最优的定量与定性表现；模型无需显式逆向渲染监督，仍能准确模拟光照与几何、材质的交互，尤其在物体内部布光、透明材料重光照等挑战性场景中表现出色。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于属性令牌的重光照方法实现了对多维光照属性的精确控制，并展现出对光照物理规律的内在理解能力，显著提升了重光照的真实感与灵活性，为数字内容创作与视觉计算提供了有力工具。

Abstract: This paper presents a method for image relighting that enables precise and continuous control over multiple illumination attributes in a photograph. We formulate relighting as a conditional image generation task and introduce attribute tokens to encode distinct lighting factors such as intensity, color, ambient illumination, diffuse level, and 3D light positions. The model is trained on a large-scale synthetic dataset with ground-truth lighting annotations, supplemented by a small set of real captures to enhance realism and generalization. We validate our approach across a variety of relighting tasks, including controlling in-scene lighting fixtures and editing environment illumination using virtual light sources, on synthetic and real images. Our method achieves state-of-the-art quantitative and qualitative performance compared to prior work. Remarkably, without explicit inverse rendering supervision, the model exhibits an inherent understanding of how light interacts with scene geometry, occlusion, and materials, yielding convincing lighting effects even in traditionally challenging scenarios such as placing lights within objects or relighting transparent materials plausibly. Project page: vrroom.github.io/tokenlight/

### [71] [LeapAlign: Post-Training Flow Matching Models at Any Generation Step by Building Two-Step Trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15311)
*Zhanhao Liang,Tao Yang,Jie Wu,Chengjian Feng,Liang Zheng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出LeapAlign方法，用于解决流匹配模型在对齐人类偏好时因长轨迹反向传播导致的内存开销大和梯度爆炸问题。通过将长轨迹缩短为两步跳跃，每步跳过多个ODE采样步骤并单步预测未来潜在状态，实现从奖励到早期生成步骤的直接梯度传播。随机化跳跃起止时间提升效率与稳定性，并通过加权策略增强与原路径一致性的轨迹贡献，同时降低大梯度项权重以提升训练稳定性。在Flux模型上的实验表明，LeapAlign优于现有GRPO和直接梯度方法，在图像质量与图文对齐方面表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接通过流匹配模型的可微生成过程进行奖励梯度反向传播是实现人类偏好对齐的有效方法，但长轨迹导致高内存消耗和梯度爆炸，使早期生成步骤难以更新，而这些步骤对最终图像结构至关重要。

Method: 提出LeapAlign方法，将长生成轨迹压缩为两个连续跳跃步骤，每个跳跃跳过多个ODE采样步骤并单步预测未来潜在状态；通过随机化跳跃起止时间提高灵活性与稳定性；引入基于一致性加权的训练策略，并对大梯度项降低权重而非完全舍弃以增强梯度稳定性。

Result: 在Flux模型上，LeapAlign在多种评估指标下均显著优于当前最先进的GRPO方法和直接梯度方法，表现出更高的图像质量与更好的图像-文本对齐能力。

Conclusion: LeapAlign成功实现了高效、稳定的梯度传播，有效解决了长轨迹反向传播中的计算瓶颈问题，显著提升了流匹配模型对人类偏好的对齐效果。

Abstract: This paper focuses on the alignment of flow matching models with human preferences. A promising way is fine-tuning by directly backpropagating reward gradients through the differentiable generation process of flow matching. However, backpropagating through long trajectories results in prohibitive memory costs and gradient explosion. Therefore, direct-gradient methods struggle to update early generation steps, which are crucial for determining the global structure of the final image. To address this issue, we introduce LeapAlign, a fine-tuning method that reduces computational cost and enables direct gradient propagation from reward to early generation steps. Specifically, we shorten the long trajectory into only two steps by designing two consecutive leaps, each skipping multiple ODE sampling steps and predicting future latents in a single step. By randomizing the start and end timesteps of the leaps, LeapAlign leads to efficient and stable model updates at any generation step. To better use such shortened trajectories, we assign higher training weights to those that are more consistent with the long generation path. To further enhance gradient stability, we reduce the weights of gradient terms with large magnitude, instead of completely removing them as done in previous works. When fine-tuning the Flux model, LeapAlign consistently outperforms state-of-the-art GRPO-based and direct-gradient methods across various metrics, achieving superior image quality and image-text alignment.

</details>

Method: 设计双向跨模态提示框架，将双模态数据映射至统一规范空间，通过双向投影融合事件与帧域的互补特征，实现精细对齐的立体表示。

Extensive experiments demonstrate that our approach significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods in accuracy and generalization.

### [74] [Decoupling Scores and Text: The Politeness Principle in Peer Review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14162)
*Yingxuan Wen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究分析了同行评审中评分与文本反馈的可靠性差异，发现基于数值评分的模型预测准确率（91%）显著高于基于文本的模型（81%），即使使用大语言模型。研究揭示了评分分布的高尖峰负偏态特征，表明个别低分对拒稿具有决定性作用；同时，文本反馈受‘礼貌原则’影响，拒绝稿件的评论仍以正面词汇为主，掩盖真实拒稿信号，导致作者难以仅凭文字判断结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者在解读同行评审反馈时常因礼貌性措辞产生误判或困惑，亟需理解评分与文本反馈在预测论文接受结果上的有效性差异。

Method: 构建包含3万余篇ICLR 2021-2025投稿的数据集，比较基于数值评分与文本评论的接受预测性能；通过分析失败样本的评分分布特征及评论情感倾向，揭示其背后机制。

Result: 评分模型准确率达91%，文本模型仅为81%；评分分布呈现高尖峰负偏态，表明个别低分起关键作用；文本评论普遍受礼貌原则影响，正向情感占优，削弱拒稿信号。

Conclusion: 数值评分比文本反馈更具预测可靠性，而文本评论因礼貌性表达掩盖真实意图，建议改进评审反馈机制以提升透明度与可解释性。

Abstract: Authors often struggle to interpret peer review feedback, deriving false hope from polite comments or feeling confused by specific low scores. To investigate this, we construct a dataset of over 30,000 ICLR 2021-2025 submissions and compare acceptance prediction performance using numerical scores versus text reviews. Our experiments reveal a significant performance gap: score-based models achieve 91% accuracy, while text-based models reach only 81% even with large language models, indicating that textual information is considerably less reliable. To explain this phenomenon, we first analyze the 9% of samples that score-based models fail to predict, finding their score distributions exhibit high kurtosis and negative skewness, which suggests that individual low scores play a decisive role in rejection even when the average score falls near the borderline. We then examine why text-based accuracy significantly lags behind scores from a review sentiment perspective, revealing the prevalence of the Politeness Principle: reviews of rejected papers still contain more positive than negative sentiment words, masking the true rejection signal and making it difficult for authors to judge outcomes from text alone.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建基于LLM的合成数据生成管道，生成包含各种挑战性变体的逼真遇险消息，将其合成语音并加入模拟噪声，再经由ASR系统转录，形成带噪真实语料用于训练与评估。

Abstract: Maritime distress communications transmitted over very high frequency (VHF) radio are safety-critical voice messages used to report emergencies at sea. Under the Global Maritime Distress and Safety System (GMDSS), such messages follow standardized procedures and are expected to convey essential details, including vessel identity, position, nature of the distress, and required assistance. In practice, however, automatic analysis remains difficult because distress messages are often brief, noisy, and produced under stress, may deviate from the prescribed format, and are further degraded by automatic speech recognition (ASR) errors caused by channel noise and speaker stress. This paper presents SeaAlert, an LLM-based framework for robust analysis of maritime distress communications. To address the scarcity of labeled real-world data, we develop a synthetic data generation pipeline in which an LLM produces realistic and diverse maritime messages, including challenging variants in which standard distress codewords are omitted or replaced with less explicit expressions. The generated utterances are synthesized into speech, degraded with simulated VHF noise, and transcribed by an ASR system to obtain realistic noisy transcripts.

### [76] [How to Fine-Tune a Reasoning Model? A Teacher-Student Cooperation Framework to Synthesize Student-Consistent SFT Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14164)
*Zixian Huang,Kaichen Yang,Xu Huang,Feiyang Hao,Qiming Ge,Bowen Li,He Du,Kai Chen,Qipeng Guo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有使用强教师模型生成合成数据进行监督微调的方法在新兴推理模型如Qwen3-8B上效果不佳，甚至导致性能下降，主要原因是教师生成数据与学生模型分布之间存在显著风格差异。

Method: 提出TESSY框架，通过交替让教师和学生模型生成风格相关与非风格相关的标记，使合成数据既保留教师的高级推理能力，又符合学生的风格分布。

Abstract: A widely adopted strategy for model enhancement is to use synthetic data generated by a stronger model for supervised fine-tuning (SFT). However, for emerging reasoning models like Qwen3-8B, this approach often fails to improve reasoning capabilities and can even lead to a substantial drop in performance. In this work, we identify substantial stylistic divergence between teacher generated data and the distribution of student as a major factor impacting SFT. To bridge this gap, we propose a Teacher-Student Cooperation Data Synthesis framework (TESSY), which interleaves teacher and student models to alternately generate style and non-style tokens. Consequently, TESSY produces synthetic sequences that inherit the advanced reasoning capabilities of the teacher while maintaining stylistic consistency with the distribution of the student. In experiments on code generation using GPT-OSS-120B as the teacher, fine-tuning Qwen3-8B on teacher-generated data leads to performance drops of 3.25% on LiveCodeBench-Pro and 10.02% on OJBench, whereas TESSY achieves improvements of 11.25% and 6.68%.

### [77] [Hierarchical Retrieval Augmented Generation for Adversarial Technique Annotation in Cyber Threat Intelligence Text](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14166)
*Filippo Morbiato,Markus Keller,Priya Nair,Luca Romano*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出H-TechniqueRAG，一种基于层次化检索的框架，通过利用MITRE ATT&CK框架中的战术-技术层级结构，显著提升威胁情报文本到技术ID映射的效率与准确性。该方法在三组不同数据集上表现优于现有最优模型，F1得分提升3.8%，推理延迟降低62.4%，API调用减少60%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计两阶段层次化检索机制：先定位宏观战术，再聚焦对应战术内的技术；引入战术感知重排序模块和层次约束的上下文组织策略，以优化生成质量并减轻大模型负担。

Result: 在三个CTI数据集上，H-TechniqueRAG相比TechniqueRAG提升3.8% F1分数，推理延迟下降62.4%，API调用减少60%，且具备更强跨域泛化能力与可解释性决策路径。

Conclusion: H-TechniqueRAG通过引入ATT&CK的层次结构作为归纳偏置，有效提升了威胁情报标注的精度、效率与可解释性，为自动化威胁防御提供了有力支持。

Abstract: Mapping Cyber Threat Intelligence (CTI) text to MITRE ATT\&CK technique IDs is a critical task for understanding adversary behaviors and automating threat defense. While recent Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) approaches have demonstrated promising capabilities in this domain, they fundamentally rely on a flat retrieval paradigm. By treating all techniques uniformly, these methods overlook the inherent taxonomy of the ATT\&CK framework, where techniques are structurally organized under high-level tactics. In this paper, we propose H-TechniqueRAG, a novel hierarchical RAG framework that injects this tactic-technique taxonomy as a strong inductive bias to achieve highly efficient and accurate annotation. Our approach introduces a two-stage hierarchical retrieval mechanism: it first identifies the macro-level tactics (the adversary's technical goals) and subsequently narrows the search to techniques within those tactics, effectively reducing the candidate search space by 77.5\%. To further bridge the gap between retrieval and generation, we design a tactic-aware reranking module and a hierarchy-constrained context organization strategy that mitigates LLM context overload and improves reasoning precision. Comprehensive experiments across three diverse CTI datasets demonstrate that H-TechniqueRAG not only outperforms the state-of-the-art TechniqueRAG by 3.8\% in F1 score, but also achieves a 62.4\% reduction in inference latency and a 60\% decrease in LLM API calls. Further analysis reveals that our hierarchical structural priors equip the model with superior cross-domain generalization and provide security analysts with highly interpretable, step-by-step decision paths.

### [80] [Stateful Evidence-Driven Retrieval-Augmented Generation with Iterative Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14170)
*Qi Dong,Ziheng Lin,Ning Ding*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于迭代推理的有状态证据驱动RAG框架，通过将检索文档转化为带有相关性和置信度信号的结构化推理单元，并在持久证据池中持续积累支持与非支持信息，实现渐进式证据累积。该框架通过证据驱动的缺陷分析识别知识缺口与冲突，迭代优化查询以引导后续检索，显著提升模型在噪声检索下的稳定性和鲁棒性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将问答建模为渐进式证据积累过程；将检索文档转换为包含显式相关性和置信度信号的结构化推理单元；维护一个持久证据池以保存支持与非支持信息；通过证据驱动的缺陷分析识别知识缺口与冲突；迭代优化查询以指导后续检索。

Conclusion: 所提出的有状态证据驱动RAG框架通过迭代推理与证据累积机制，克服了传统RAG的局限性，实现了更稳定、更可靠的问答表现，尤其适用于高噪声环境下的知识增强任务。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) grounds Large Language Models (LLMs) in external knowledge but often suffers from flat context representations and stateless retrieval, leading to unstable performance. We propose Stateful Evidence-Driven RAG with Iterative Reasoning, a framework that models question answering as a progressive evidence accumulation process. Retrieved documents are converted into structured reasoning units with explicit relevance and confidence signals and maintained in a persistent evidence pool capturing both supportive and non-supportive information. The framework performs evidence-driven deficiency analysis to identify gaps and conflicts and iteratively refines queries to guide subsequent retrieval. This iterative reasoning process enables stable evidence aggregation and improves robustness to noisy retrieval. Experiments on multiple question answering benchmarks demonstrate consistent improvements over standard RAG and multi-step baselines, while effectively accumulating high-quality evidence and maintaining stable performance under substantial retrieval noise.

### [81] [Benchmarking Linguistic Adaptation in Comparable-Sized LLMs: A Study of Llama-3.1-8B, Mistral-7B-v0.1, and Qwen3-8B on Romanized Nepali](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14171)
*Ananda Rimal,Adarsha Rimal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究首次系统性地评估了三个可比规模的开源大模型（Llama-3.1-8B、Mistral-7B-v0.1、Qwen3-8B）在罗马化尼泊尔语上的语言适应能力，基于10,000个双语指令跟随样本数据集，在零样本和微调设置下进行测试。通过困惑度（PPL）、BERTScore、chrF++等七项指标衡量流畅性、语音一致性与语义完整性。采用QLoRA结合rsLoRA方法在双NVIDIA Tesla T4 GPU上仅微调约1%参数，总训练时间少于27小时。零样本下三模型均无法生成罗马化尼泊尔语，且呈现架构特异性失败模式；微调后全部解决该问题，平均BERTScore达0.75，chrF++超过23。综合十项标准评估表明，Qwen3-8B为最优架构，其在零样本即能生成语义相关输出，并在结构对齐指标上领先。同时验证‘适应潜力假设’：尽管Llama-3.1-8B零样本表现最差，但其在微调后取得最大提升（PPL下降49.77，BERTScore上升0.3287），适合低资源迭代开发流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 罗马化尼泊尔语作为尼泊尔非正式数字交流的主要媒介，但在大型语言模型领域仍严重缺乏资源支持。现有模型在该语言上的表现尚无系统评估，亟需建立基准以推动低资源语言的适配研究。

Method: 构建包含10,000条罗马化尼泊尔语指令样本的双语数据集，对Llama-3.1-8B、Mistral-7B-v0.1、Qwen3-8B三模型在零样本与微调条件下进行评估。使用量化低秩自适应（QLoRA）结合秩稳定LoRA（rsLoRA）在双Tesla T4 GPU上微调，仅训练约1%参数，耗时<27小时。性能评估涵盖五项指标、七项测量维度。

Result: 零样本阶段三模型均无法生成罗马化尼泊尔语，表现出不同架构特异性失败模式；微调后所有模型成功生成，平均BERTScore达0.75，chrF++ > 23。Qwen3-8B在零样本即具备语义相关输出能力，且在结构对齐指标中领先。Llama-3.1-8B虽初始表现最差，但微调后提升幅度最大（PPL下降49.77，BERTScore上升0.3287）。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了首个针对可比规模开源大模型在罗马化尼泊尔语上的严谨基准。结果表明，尽管各模型初始表现差异显著，但通过轻量级微调可有效实现语言适配。Qwen3-8B在整体性能上最优，而Llama-3.1-8B展现出最大适应潜力，适用于迭代式低资源开发流程。

Abstract: Romanized Nepali, the Nepali language written in the Latin alphabet, is the dominant medium for informal digital communication in Nepal, yet it remains critically underresourced in the landscape of Large Language Models (LLMs). This study presents a systematic benchmarking of linguistic adaptation across three comparable-sized open-weight models: Llama-3.1-8B, Mistral-7B-v0.1, and Qwen3-8B. We evaluate these architectures under zero-shot and fine-tuned settings using a curated bilingual dataset of 10,000 transliterated instruction-following samples. Performance is quantified across five metrics spanning seven measurement dimensions: Perplexity (PPL), BERTScore, chrF++, ROUGE-1, ROUGE-2, ROUGE-L, and BLEU, capturing fluency, phonetic consistency, and semantic integrity. Models were fine-tuned using Quantized Low-Rank Adaptation (QLoRA) with Rank-Stabilized LoRA (rsLoRA) at rank r=32 on dual NVIDIA Tesla T4 GPUs, training only approximately 1% of each model's parameters in under 27 total GPU-hours. At zero-shot, all three models fail to generate Romanized Nepali, each exhibiting a distinct architecture-specific failure mode. Following fine-tuning, all three resolve these failures and converge to BERTScore approximately 0.75 and chrF++ greater than 23. Overall dimension-wise assessment across ten criteria identifies Qwen3-8B as the overall recommended architecture, being the only model to produce semantically relevant zero-shot output and leading all structural alignment metrics post-SFT. The adaptation headroom hypothesis is confirmed: Llama-3.1-8B, despite its weakest zero-shot baseline, achieves the largest absolute fine-tuning gains in PPL (Delta = -49.77) and BERTScore (Delta = +0.3287), making it the preferred choice for iterative low-resource development pipelines. This work establishes the first rigorous baseline for Romanized Nepali adaptation in comparable-sized open-weight LLMs.

### [82] [Correcting Suppressed Log-Probabilities in Language Models with Post-Transformer Adapters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14174)
*Bryan Sanchez*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种小型后变压器适配器（786K参数），可纠正语言模型在政治敏感话题上抑制事实概率的问题。该适配器在冻结的隐藏状态上训练，能有效恢复31个意识形态区分性事实的生成概率，在不同规模的Qwen3模型中表现良好。适配器在训练数据上实现记忆，并在未见数据上泛化至11-39%。使用门控（SwiGLU）和非门控（线性瓶颈）结构效果相当，且均不显著优于对方。仅在当前预测位置应用适配器时，可生成连贯、较少被压制的内容；若在整个生成过程中应用，则导致输出不连贯。基于对数空间的适配器在任何模式下均无法生成连贯文本，表明隐藏状态干预是修正生成的关键层级。此外，文中揭示了Apple MLX中一个此前未记录的静默梯度错误，解释了前期实验中所有失败结果，并提供了最小复现方案及对适配器研究的启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对齐调优的语言模型在政治敏感话题上虽保留知识但抑制事实生成概率，亟需一种高效、可迁移的方法来修复此类偏差，同时避免破坏生成连贯性。

Method: 设计并训练一个小型后变压器适配器，作用于冻结的隐藏状态；通过锚定训练实现零知识回归；对比门控与非门控结构；测试不同应用位置（全序列 vs. 仅最后位置）对生成质量的影响；评估对数空间适配器的表现；发现并验证MLX中的梯度错误。

Result: 适配器在31个敏感事实中成功恢复真实概率，训练集完全记忆，跨5次随机划分泛化率11–39%；门控与非门控性能相近；仅在最后位置应用时生成连贯内容；对数空间适配器无效；揭示并修复了MLX中导致早期失败的梯度错误。

Conclusion: 隐藏状态层面的轻量级适配器是纠正语言模型政治敏感话题压制的有效方法；适配器设计应限制在当前预测位置以维持连贯性；框架中存在关键工具链缺陷，需警惕其对实验结果的影响。

Abstract: Alignment-tuned language models frequently suppress factual log-probabilities on politically sensitive topics despite retaining the knowledge in their hidden representations. We show that a 786K-parameter (approximately 0.02% of the base model) post-transformer adapter, trained on frozen hidden states, corrects this suppression on 31 ideology-discriminating facts across Qwen3-4B, 8B, and 14B. The adapter memorizes all 15 training facts and generalizes to 11--39% of 16 held-out facts across 5 random splits per scale, with zero knowledge regressions via anchored training. Both gated (SwiGLU) and ungated (linear bottleneck) adapters achieve comparable results; neither consistently outperforms the other (Fisher exact p > 0.09 at all scales). On instruct models, the adapter corrects log-probability rankings. When applied at all token positions during generation, the adapter produces incoherent output; however, when applied only at the current prediction position (last-position-only), the adapter produces coherent, less censored text. A logit-space adapter operating after token projection fails to produce coherent generation at any application mode, suggesting hidden-state intervention is the correct level for generation correction. A previously undocumented silent gradient bug in Apple MLX explains all null results in earlier iterations of this work: the standard pattern nn.value_and_grad(model, fn)(model.parameters()) returns zero gradients without error; the correct pattern nn.value_and_grad(model, fn)(model, data) resolves this. We provide a minimal reproduction and discuss implications for other adapter research using MLX.

### [83] [QU-NLP at ArchEHR-QA 2026: Two-Stage QLoRA Fine-Tuning of Qwen3-4B for Patient-Oriented Clinical Question Answering and Evidence Sentence Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14175)
*Mohammad AL-Smadi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统一系统，同时解决ArchEHR-QA共享任务中的子任务3（答案生成）和子任务4（证据句对齐）。针对子任务3，采用两阶段量化低秩微调（QLoRA）在4位NF4量化下对Qwen3-4B模型进行训练，先在emrQA-MedSQuAD语料库的3万样本上建立临床领域能力，再在20个标注开发案例上学习任务特定输出风格，最终在官方测试集上取得综合得分32.87（BLEU=9.42, ROUGE-L=27.04, SARI=55.42, BERTScore=43.00, AlignScore=25.28, MEDCON=37.04）。针对子任务4，构建了三种检索方法的加权集成：带相对阈值的BM25、TF-IDF余弦相似度及微调的交叉编码器，用于识别支持给定答案的病历句子，在100个案例测试集上达到微平均F1为67.16。实验表明，两个子任务均暴露同一根本挑战：仅20个标注训练案例不足以区分相关与无关临床句子，提示数据增强是未来最具提升潜力的方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前临床问答系统在答案生成与证据句对齐方面仍面临挑战，尤其在有限标注数据条件下难以有效区分相关与无关的临床信息。本研究旨在通过高效微调与集成检索策略，提升系统在真实医疗场景下的表现，并揭示数据稀缺的根本性问题。

Method: 对于子任务3，采用两阶段量化低秩微调（QLoRA）策略：首先在大规模临床语料emrQA-MedSQuAD的3万样本上预训练以建立领域知识；随后在20个标注开发案例上进行第二阶段微调，以适配任务特定输出风格。模型基于4位NF4量化下的Qwen3-4B。对于子任务4，设计加权集成检索框架，结合BM25（带相对阈值）、TF-IDF余弦相似度与微调的交叉编码器，筛选支持答案的关键病历句子。

Result: 子任务3在测试集上获得综合得分32.87，具体指标包括：BLEU=9.42，ROUGE-L=27.04，SARI=55.42，BERTScore=43.00，AlignScore=25.28，MEDCON=37.04。子任务4在100例测试集上实现微平均F1为67.16。实验进一步发现，仅20个标注样本无法有效区分相关与无关临床句子，凸显数据量不足的瓶颈。

Conclusion: 尽管所提系统在两个子任务上均取得了良好表现，但实验结果一致指向一个核心问题：少量标注数据限制了模型对临床相关信息的精准识别。因此，未来工作应优先聚焦于数据增强策略，以显著提升系统的泛化能力与鲁棒性。

Abstract: We present a unified system addressing both Subtask 3 (answer generation) and Subtask 4 (evidence sentence alignment) of the ArchEHR-QA Shared Task. For Subtask 3, we apply two-stage Quantised Low-Rank Adaptation (QLoRA) to Qwen3-4B loaded in 4-bit NF4 quantisation: first on 30,000 samples from the emrQA-MedSQuAD corpus to establish clinical domain competence, then on the 20 annotated development cases to learn the task-specific output style. Our system achieves an overall score of 32.87 on the official test-2026 split (BLEU = 9.42, ROUGE-L = 27.04, SARI = 55.42, BERTScore = 43.00, AlignScore = 25.28, MEDCON = 37.04). For Subtask 4, we develop a weighted ensemble of three retrieval methods - BM25 with relative thresholding, TF-IDF cosine similarity, and a fine-tuned cross-encoder - to identify note sentences supporting a given gold answer, achieving a micro-F1 of 67.16 on the 100-case test set. Experiments reveal that both subtasks expose the same fundamental challenge: 20 annotated training cases are insufficient to distinguish relevant from irrelevant clinical sentences, pointing to data augmentation as the highest-leverage future direction.

### [84] [Listen, Correct, and Feed Back: Spoken Pedagogical Feedback Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14177)
*Junhong Liang,Yifan Lu,Ekaterina Kochmar,Fajri Koto*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出SPFG数据集，用于生成口语化、教学友好的语法错误纠正反馈；在SGEC任务中评估三个指令微调大模型，比较SFT与基于偏好的对齐方法（DPO/KTO），发现SFT表现更稳定，纠错与反馈质量弱相关，代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语法错误纠正与解释研究虽进展迅速，但在真实教学场景中仍缺乏可操作、适合学习者水平且鼓励性的教师式反馈，亟需构建面向教学的高质量反馈生成体系。

Method: 基于Speak & Improve Challenge 2025语料构建SPFG数据集，包含流畅性转录、语法纠错目标及人工验证的教师风格反馈（含偏好对）；采用指令微调的大模型（Qwen2.5、Llama-3.1、GLM-4）在转录基础上进行口语语法纠错，并对比监督微调（SFT）与基于偏好对齐的方法（DPO、KTO）联合生成纠错结果与反馈。

Result: SFT在纠错与反馈生成上表现最一致且效果最佳，而DPO/KTO带来的提升较小或不稳定；纠错质量与反馈质量之间呈现弱相关性，表明两者可独立优化。

Conclusion: SPFG数据集有效支持了口语化教学反馈生成任务；实验表明，监督微调优于基于偏好的对齐方法，且纠错与反馈生成可解耦优化，为未来智能教学系统设计提供了实践依据。

Abstract: Grammatical error correction (GEC) and explanation (GEE) have made rapid progress, but real teaching scenarios also require \emph{learner-friendly pedagogical feedback} that is actionable, level-appropriate, and encouraging. We introduce \textbf{SPFG} (\textbf{S}poken \textbf{P}edagogical \textbf{F}eedback \textbf{G}eneration), a dataset built based on the Speak \& Improve Challenge 2025 corpus, pairing fluency-oriented transcriptions with GEC targets and \emph{human-verified} teacher-style feedback, including preferred/rejected feedback pairs for preference learning. We study a transcript-based Spoken Grammatical Error Correction (SGEC) setting and evaluate three instruction-tuned LLMs (Qwen2.5, Llama-3.1, and GLM-4), comparing supervised fine-tuning (SFT) with preference-based alignment (using DPO and KTO) for jointly generating corrections and feedback. Results show that SFT provides the most consistent improvements, while DPO/KTO yield smaller or mixed gains, and that correction quality and feedback quality are weakly coupled. Our implementation is available at https://github.com/Skywalker-Harrison/spfg.

</details>


### [85] [An Underexplored Frontier: Large Language Models for Rare Disease Patient Education and Communication -- A scoping review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14179)
*Zaifu Zhan,Yu Hou,Kai Yu,Min Zeng,Anita Burgun,Xiaoyi Chen,Rui Zhang*

Result: 现有研究高度集中于近期成果，以通用模型为主（如ChatGPT），聚焦于预设问题集的问答任务；缺乏真实世界数据与长期沟通场景的应用；评估标准以准确性为核心，对可读性、共情能力、沟通质量等患者中心指标关注不足；多语言支持极为有限。

Conclusion: 该领域仍处于早期发展阶段。未来研究应优先推动以患者为中心的设计、领域自适应方法，并注重真实环境中的部署，以构建安全、灵活且高效的罕见病沟通支持体系。

Abstract: Rare diseases affect over 300 million people worldwide and are characterized by complex care pathways, limited clinical expertise, and substantial unmet communication needs throughout the long patient journey. Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) offer new opportunities to support patient education and communication, yet their application in rare diseases remains unclear.
  We conducted a scoping review of studies published between January 2022 and March 2026 across major databases, identifying 12 studies on LLM-based rare disease patient education and communication. Most studies focus on patient question answering using curated question sets, with limited use of real-world data or longitudinal communication scenarios. Evaluations are primarily centered on accuracy, with limited attention to patient-centered dimensions such as readability, empathy, and communication quality.   Overall, the field remains at an early stage. Future research should prioritize patient-centered design, domain-adapted methods, and real-world deployment to support safe, adaptive, and effective communication in rare diseases.

### [86] [Internal Knowledge Without External Expression: Probing the Generalization Boundary of a Classical Chinese Language Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14180)
*Jiuting Chen,Yuan Lian,Hao Wu,Tianqi Huang,Hiroshi Sasaki,Makoto Kouno,Jongil Choi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究训练了一个318M参数的Transformer语言模型，仅使用15.6亿词的纯文言文语料，无英文字符或阿拉伯数字。通过分布外（OOD）测试发现，模型在内部能区分真实与虚构历史事件（困惑度提升2.39倍），但无法在生成文本中表达不确定性；文言文中表不确定性的标记在OOD问题中出现频率反而更低（3.5% vs 8.3%）。这一现象在中、英、日三种语言及多个规模模型中重复验证。研究指出，元认知表达（如‘我不知道’）不会仅通过语言建模自发产生，需显式训练信号（如强化学习人类反馈）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大规模语言模型是否具备真正的元认知能力，即能否在面对未知信息时识别并表达不确定性，尤其是在纯文言文等非现代语言环境中。

Method: 在纯文言文语料上从零训练318M参数Transformer模型；设计真实、虚构和半虚构历史事件作为测试样本；通过困惑度分析内部不确定性感知；统计生成文本中表不确定性的语言标记频率，比较分布内与分布外输入的表现；跨语言、跨模型规模复现结果。

Result: 模型内部表现出对事实真伪的敏感性（困惑度显著上升），但外部生成中却极少表达不确定性，甚至在未知输入下使用更少的怀疑性语言标记；不同语言模型中不确定性表达模式受训练数据惯例影响，存在‘谦逊悖论’（文言文）与几乎不使用推测标记（日语）的现象。

Conclusion: 语言建模本身不足以催生真正的元认知表达能力，模型无法自发学会说‘我不知道’。要实现可信的不确定性表达，必须引入如强化学习人类反馈（RLHF）等显式训练机制。

Abstract: We train a 318M-parameter Transformer language model from scratch on a curated corpus of 1.56 billion tokens of pure Classical Chinese, with zero English characters or Arabic numerals. Through systematic out-of-distribution (OOD) testing, we investigate whether the model can distinguish known from unknown inputs, and crucially, whether it can express this distinction in its generated text.
  We find a clear dissociation between internal and external uncertainty. Internally, the model exhibits a perplexity jump ratio of 2.39x between real and fabricated historical events (p = 8.9e-11, n = 92 per group), with semi-fabricated events (real figures + fictional events) showing the highest perplexity (4.24x, p = 1.1e-16), demonstrating genuine factual encoding beyond syntactic pattern matching. Externally, however, the model never learns to express uncertainty: classical Chinese epistemic markers appear at lower rates for OOD questions (3.5%) than for in-distribution questions (8.3%, p = 0.023), reflecting rhetorical conventions rather than genuine metacognition.
  We replicate both findings across three languages (Classical Chinese, English, Japanese), three writing systems, and eight models from 110M to 1.56B parameters. We further show that uncertainty expression frequency is determined entirely by training data conventions, with Classical Chinese models showing a "humility paradox" (more hedging for known topics), while Japanese models almost never hedge. We argue that metacognitive expression -- the ability to say "I don't know" -- does not emerge from language modeling alone and requires explicit training signals such as RLHF.

</details>


### [87] [The PICCO Framework for Large Language Model Prompting: A Taxonomy and Reference Architecture for Prompt Structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14197)
*David A. Cook*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出PICCO框架，通过整合11个已有提示框架，构建了一个五元素的参考架构（角色、指令、上下文、约束、输出），旨在提升提示设计的概念清晰度与系统性。同时区分了提示框架、元素、生成、技术与工程等概念，并总结了相关实现概念与未来研究方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型的性能高度依赖于提示设计，但提示构建在描述和应用上存在不一致问题，亟需一个统一、清晰的参考框架以促进系统化提示设计。

Method: 通过多数据库检索识别11个已有提示框架，并进行严谨的综合分析，提炼出概念分类与五元素参考架构。

Result: 提出并验证了PICCO框架，明确了各元素的功能、范围及其相互关系，为提示设计提供了结构化指导；同时梳理了关键实施概念与未来研究方向。

Conclusion: PICCO是一个概念性与方法论贡献，旨在标准化提示规范与比较，但未对框架本身进行实证验证。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) performance depends heavily on prompt design, yet prompt construction is often described and applied inconsistently. Our purpose was to derive a reference framework for structuring LLM prompts. This paper presents PICCO, a framework derived through a rigorous synthesis of 11 previously published prompting frameworks identified through a multi-database search. The analysis yields two main contributions. First, it proposes a taxonomy that distinguishes prompt frameworks, prompt elements, prompt generation, prompting techniques, and prompt engineering as related but non-equivalent concepts. Second, it derives a five-element reference architecture for prompt generation: Persona, Instructions, Context, Constraints, and Output (PICCO). For each element, we define its function, scope, and relationship to other elements, with the goal of improving conceptual clarity and supporting more systematic prompt design. Finally, to support application of the framework, we outline key concepts relevant to implementation, including prompting techniques (e.g., zero-shot, few-shot, chain-of-thought, ensembling, decomposition, and self-critique, with selected variants), human and automated approaches to iterative prompt engineering, responsible prompting considerations such as security, privacy, bias, and trust, and priorities for future research. This work is a conceptual and methodological contribution: it formalizes a common structure for prompt specification and comparison, but does not claim empirical validation of PICCO as an optimization method.

### [88] [Chinese Language Is Not More Efficient Than English in Vibe Coding: A Preliminary Study on Token Cost and Problem-Solving Rate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14210)
*Simiao Ren,Xingyu Shen,Yuchen Zhou,Dennis,Ng,Ankit Raj*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过SWE-bench Lite基准对中文与英文提示在大语言模型编码任务中的效率进行了实证分析，发现中文提示并未表现出预期的token效率优势，部分模型（如MiniMax-2.7）甚至消耗更多token，而另一些模型（如GLM-5）虽减少token使用但任务成功率更低。综合考虑token成本与任务成功率，中文提示并未带来成本节约或性能提升。研究结果表明，语言对token成本的影响具有模型依赖性，不应仅因语言切换而期望成本降低或效果提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社交媒体和实践者论坛中流传着‘中文提示比英文更节省token，可降低高达40%成本’的说法，影响开发者选择中文进行‘vibe coding’以节省API开支。该说法缺乏严谨验证，亟需实证研究检验其有效性。

Method: 采用SWE-bench Lite这一软件工程任务基准，对多个大语言模型在中文与英文提示下的token消耗、任务成功率及成本效率进行对比实验，系统评估语言对提示效率的影响。

Result: 1. 中文提示未表现出token效率优势；2. 不同模型对语言的响应差异显著：MiniMax-2.7中文提示增加1.28倍token消耗，而GLM-5则减少；3. 所有模型在中文提示下的任务成功率普遍低于英文；4. 综合任务成功与token成本的成本效率分析显示，中文提示未带来实际成本节约。

Conclusion: 语言对token成本的影响高度依赖模型架构，不能一概而论。当前证据表明，单纯切换至中文提示并不能实现成本节省或性能提升，开发者应谨慎对待此类传言，避免基于未经验证的假设做出决策。

Abstract: A claim has been circulating on social media and practitioner forums that Chinese prompts are more token-efficient than English for LLM coding tasks, potentially reducing costs by up to 40\%. This claim has influenced developers to consider switching to Chinese for ``vibe coding'' to save on API costs. In this paper, we conduct a rigorous empirical study using SWE-bench Lite, a benchmark of software engineering tasks, to evaluate whether this claim of Chinese token efficiency holds up to scrutiny. Our results reveal three key findings: First, the efficiency advantage of Chinese is not observed. Second, token cost varies by model architecture in ways that defy simple assumptions: while MiniMax-2.7 shows 1.28x higher token costs for Chinese, GLM-5 actually consumes fewer tokens with Chinese prompts. Third, and most importantly, we found that the success rate when prompting in Chinese is generally lower than in English across all models we tested. We also measure cost efficiency as expected cost per successful task -- jointly accounting for token consumption and task resolution rate. These findings should be interpreted as preliminary evidence rather than a definitive conclusion, given the limited number of models evaluated and the narrow set of benchmarks tested due to resource constraints; they indicate that language effects on token cost are model-dependent, and that practitioners should not expect cost savings or performance gains just by switching their prompt language to Chinese.

### [89] [ReviewGrounder: Improving Review Substantiveness with Rubric-Guided, Tool-Integrated Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14261)
*Zhuofeng Li,Yi Lu,Dongfu Jiang,Haoxiang Zhang,Yuyang Bai,Chuan Li,Yu Wang,Shuiwang Ji,Jianwen Xie,Yu Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究针对大语言模型（LLM）在学术同行评审中生成内容肤浅、缺乏实质性证据的问题，提出REVIEWBENCH基准和REVIEWGROUNDER框架。REVIEWBENCH通过论文特定的评分标准评估评论质量，而REVIEWGROUNDER采用分阶段的多智能体架构，结合显式评分标准与上下文证据整合，显著提升评论深度与准确性。实验表明，即使使用较小模型作为起草者，其性能也优于大型基线模型（如GPT-4.1、DeepSeek-R1-670B），在8个维度上更贴近人类判断。代码已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在学术评审中生成的反馈常为表面化、模板化，缺乏基于证据的实质性意见，主要因未有效利用人类评审中的显式评分标准和对已有工作的上下文依赖。

Method: 提出REVIEWBENCH基准，用于评估评论是否符合论文特定的评分标准；设计REVIEWGROUNDER框架，包含草案生成与上下文证据强化两个阶段，通过多智能体协作实现基于评分标准的精准反馈生成。

Result: 在REVIEWBENCH上，REVIEWGROUNDER在8个维度上的评分质量及与人类判断的一致性均显著优于现有主流模型，包括使用更大规模基座模型的对比方案。

Conclusion: 通过引入结构化评分标准与上下文证据整合机制，REVIEWGROUNDER有效提升了LLM生成评审意见的质量，证明了方法设计的重要性超越单纯模型规模。

Abstract: The rapid rise in AI conference submissions has driven increasing exploration of large language models (LLMs) for peer review support. However, LLM-based reviewers often generate superficial, formulaic comments lacking substantive, evidence-grounded feedback. We attribute this to the underutilization of two key components of human reviewing: explicit rubrics and contextual grounding in existing work. To address this, we introduce REVIEWBENCH, a benchmark evaluating review text according to paper-specific rubrics derived from official guidelines, the paper's content, and human-written reviews. We further propose REVIEWGROUNDER, a rubric-guided, tool-integrated multi-agent framework that decomposes reviewing into drafting and grounding stages, enriching shallow drafts via targeted evidence consolidation. Experiments on REVIEWBENCH show that REVIEWGROUNDER, using a Phi-4-14B-based drafter and a GPT-OSS-120B-based grounding stage, consistently outperforms baselines with substantially stronger/larger backbones (e.g., GPT-4.1 and DeepSeek-R1-670B) in both alignment with human judgments and rubric-based review quality across 8 dimensions. The code is available \href{https://github.com/EigenTom/ReviewGrounder}{here}.

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated high proficiency on English-centric medical examinations, their performance often declines when faced with non-English languages and multimodal diagnostic tasks. Following FAIR data principles and SPIRIT-AI guidelines, we describe a rigorous curation process and an automated translation pipeline for comparative analysis. We evaluate contemporary multimodal LLMs using a zero-shot, strictly constrained prompting strategy to assess cross-lingual transfer and visual reasoning. EuropeMedQA aims to provide a contamination-resistant benchmark that reflects the complexity of European clinical practices and fosters the development of more generalizable medical AI.

### [91] [Tracking the Temporal Dynamics of News Coverage of Catastrophic and Violent Events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14315)
*Emily Lugos,Maurício Gruppi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究利用126,602篇在线新闻文章，分析暴力和灾难性事件报道的时空与语义动态，发现重大事件引发的新闻周期具有可预测模式：报道量迅速上升、早期语义漂移明显、随后逐渐回落至基线水平，并识别出驱动这些时间模式的关键术语。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于大规模新闻语料库，通过发布量、语义漂移、语义分散度和术语相关性等指标量化叙事变化，结合时间序列分析与自然语言处理技术进行建模与验证。

Result: 研究揭示了突发重大事件的新闻周期呈现结构化且可预测的特征，包括报道量的快速激增、早期显著的语义漂移以及后期趋于平稳的下降趋势；同时识别出在不同阶段主导叙事演变的核心关键词。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解新闻媒体在危机中的动态反应提供了数据驱动的框架，有助于更深入地把握公众舆论的生成机制与信息传播规律。

Abstract: The modern news cycle has been fundamentally reshaped by the rapid exchange of information online. As a result, media framing shifts dynamically as new information, political responses, and social reactions emerge. Understanding how these narratives form, propagate, and evolve is essential for interpreting public discourse during moments of crisis. In this study, we examine the temporal and semantic dynamics of reporting for violent and catastrophic events using a large-scale corpus of 126,602 news articles collected from online publishers. We quantify narrative change through publication volume, semantic drift, semantic dispersion, and term relevance. Our results show that sudden events of impact exhibit structured and predictable news-cycle patterns characterized by rapid surges in coverage, early semantic drift, and gradual declines toward the baseline. In addition, our results indicate the terms that are driving the temporal patterns.

### [92] [LLM Predictive Scoring and Validation: Inferring Experience Ratings from Unstructured Text](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14321)
*Jason Potteiger,Andrew Hong,Ito Zapata*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究利用GPT-4.1分析约10,000名棒球迷的开放性文字反馈，预测其在0-10分制下的观赛体验评分。结果显示，约67%的预测值与实际评分相差不超过1分，36%完全匹配；三次独立评分中预测一致性极高（87%一致，99.9%在±1分内）。预测评分与整体体验相关性最强（r=0.82），但系统性地比自评低约1分，反映出预测值捕捉的是显著情绪或难忘事件的影响，而自评则反映整体综合判断。两者差异体现不同心理构念，而非误差，具有解释价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究如何从球迷的开放性文字描述中自动预测其整体观赛体验评分，并理解预测值与自评之间的系统性差异背后的心理机制。

Method: 使用GPT-4.1对球迷提供的单条开放性文本进行评分预测，基于约10,000份来自五支MLB球队的真实调查数据，通过多次独立评分验证模型稳定性，并对比预测值与自评值的相关性和偏差。

Result: 预测评分与真实评分高度一致（67%在±1分内，36%精确匹配），且三次独立评分间一致性极高；预测值与整体体验高度相关（r=0.82），但系统性偏低约1分；该差距源于预测聚焦于显著情感事件，而自评反映整体综合判断，二者互补。

Conclusion: 一个未经优化的提示即可有效方向性预测球迷体验评分；预测值与自评之间的差距并非错误，而是反映了不同心理构念——前者捕捉关键情绪时刻，后者反映整体评价，这种差异应被保留并加以解释，具有理论和实践意义。

Abstract: We tasked GPT-4.1 to read what baseball fans wrote about their game-day experience and predict the overall experience rating each fan gave on a 0-10 survey scale. The model received only the text of a single open-ended response. These AI predictions were compared with the actual experience ratings captured by the survey instrument across approximately 10,000 fan responses from five Major League Baseball teams. In total two-thirds of predicted ratings fell within one point of self-reported fan ratings (67% within +/-1, 36% exact match), and the predicted measurement was near-deterministic across three independent scoring runs (87% exact agreement, 99.9% within +/-1). Predicted ratings aligned most strongly with the overall experience rating (r = 0.82) rather than with any specific aspect of the game-day experience such as parking, concessions, staff, etc. However, predictions were systematically lower than self-reported ratings by approximately one point, and this gap was not driven by any single aspect. Rather, our analysis shows that self-reported ratings capture the fan's verdict, an overall evaluative judgment that integrates the entire experience. While predicted ratings quantify the impact of salient moments characterized as memorable, emotionally intense, unusual, or actionable. Each measure contains information the other misses. These baseline results establish that a simple, unoptimized prompt can directionally predict how fans rate their experience from the text a fan wrote and that a gap between the two numbers can be interpreted as a construct difference worth preserving rather than an error to eliminate.

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有拒绝回答微调方法因直接按响应准确率划分数据集，导致决策边界附近存在严重标签噪声，引发高拒绝率或幻觉现象。

Method: 从潜在空间表示视角出发，揭示决策超平面附近的‘灰区’是性能瓶颈；利用线性探测构建真值超平面，并以几何距离作为置信度信号进行几何去噪，过滤模糊样本，保留高质量信号用于微调。

Result: 在Llama3、Qwen3等多个模型及TriviaQA、NQ、SciQ、SimpleQA等数据集上，GeoDe显著提升模型真实性，且在分布外（OOD）场景下表现出强泛化能力。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) often exhibit hallucinations due to their inability to accurately perceive their own knowledge boundaries. Existing abstention fine-tuning methods typically partition datasets directly based on response accuracy, causing models to suffer from severe label noise near the decision boundaries and consequently exhibit high rates of abstentions or hallucinations. This paper adopts a latent space representation perspective, revealing a "gray zone" near the decision hyperplane where internal belief ambiguity constitutes the core performance bottleneck. Based on this insight, we propose the **GeoDe** (**Geo**metric **De**noising) framework for abstention fine-tuning. This method constructs a truth hyperplane using linear probes and performs "geometric denoising" by employing geometric distance as a confidence signal for abstention decisions. This approach filters out ambiguous boundary samples while retaining high-fidelity signals for fine-tuning. Experiments across multiple models (Llama3, Qwen3) and benchmark datasets (TriviaQA, NQ, SciQ, SimpleQA) demonstrate that GeoDe significantly enhances model truthfulness and demonstrates strong generalization in out-of-distribution (OOD) scenarios. Code is available at https://github.com/Notbesidemoon/GeoDe.

### [94] [Faithfulness Serum: Mitigating the Faithfulness Gap in Textual Explanations of LLM Decisions via Attribution Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14325)
*Bar Alon,Itamar Zimerman,Lior Wolf*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文研究大语言模型（LLMs）生成的解释在认知上的忠实性问题，发现现有方法生成的解释往往缺乏对模型实际决策依据的真实反映。为此，提出一种无需训练的方法，通过注意力层面的干预，结合基于可信归因方法提取的词元级热图，显著提升解释的内在忠实性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型虽然性能强大，但其决策过程缺乏可解释性，限制了在需要透明度和信任的领域应用。现有方法生成的解释虽看似合理，但未必真实反映模型内部依赖的证据，因此亟需提升解释的内在忠实性。

Method: 提出一种无需训练的方法，利用可信归因方法获取词元级热图，并基于这些热图在注意力层面对解释生成进行干预，以引导模型生成更忠实于其实际决策依据的解释。

Result: 该方法在多个模型、基准测试和提示设置下均显著提升了解释的 epistemic faithfulness，证明了其有效性与通用性。

Conclusion: 当前的 LLM 解释方法在认知忠实性上存在不足；所提出的注意力干预方法能够有效提升解释的真实性，为构建可信赖的 AI 系统提供了新路径。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) achieve strong performance and have revolutionized NLP, but their lack of explainability keeps them treated as black boxes, limiting their use in domains that demand transparency and trust. A promising direction to address this issue is post-hoc text-based explanations, which aim to explain model decisions in natural language. Prior work has focused on generating convincing rationales that appear to be subjectively faithful, but it remains unclear whether these explanations are epistemically faithful, whether they reflect the internal evidence the model actually relied on for its decision. In this paper, we first assess the epistemic faithfulness of LLM-generated explanations via counterfactuals and show that they are often unfaithful. We then introduce a training-free method that enhances faithfulness by guiding explanation generation through attention-level interventions, informed by token-level heatmaps extracted via a faithful attribution method. This method significantly improves epistemic faithfulness across multiple models, benchmarks, and prompts.

### [95] [Shuffle the Context: RoPE-Perturbed Self-Distillation for Long-Context Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14339)
*Zichong Li,Chen Liang,Liliang Ren,Tuo Zhao,Yelong Shen,Weizhu Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出RoPE-Perturbed Self-Distillation训练正则化方法，以提升大语言模型在长上下文任务中的位置鲁棒性。通过扰动RoPE索引生成同一序列的不同“视角”，并利用自蒸馏使模型在不同位置配置下保持一致预测，从而减少对位置的依赖，增强语义理解能力。实验表明，在Llama-3-8B和Qwen-3-4B上均取得显著性能提升，最长达12.04%的准确率增益，并改善了超出训练窗口的长度外推能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长上下文适应方法在处理长文本时仍存在对证据位置敏感的问题，即使控制任务难度与格式，模型表现仍受绝对位置影响，表现出高位置方差，亟需提升模型的位置鲁棒性。

Method: 提出RoPE-Perturbed Self-Distillation方法，通过扰动输入序列的RoPE（旋转位置编码）索引，生成多个不同位置分布的视图，利用自蒸馏机制促使模型在不同视图间输出一致预测，从而学习更稳定的语义表示而非依赖位置信息。

Result: 在RULER-64K和RULER-256K等长上下文基准测试中，Llama-3-8B和Qwen-3-4B均获得显著提升，最大提升达12.04%（Llama-3-8B on RULER-64K）和2.71%（Qwen-3-4B on RULER-256K），且在超出训练长度的场景中表现出更强的外推能力。

Conclusion: RoPE-Perturbed Self-Distillation有效提升了大语言模型在长上下文任务中的位置鲁棒性，通过引入基于位置编码扰动的自蒸馏机制，使模型更依赖于语义内容而非位置线索，为长序列理解提供了高效、可扩展的训练策略。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) increasingly operate in settings that require reliable long-context understanding, such as retrieval-augmented generation and multi-document reasoning. A common strategy is to fine-tune pretrained short-context models at the target sequence length. However, we find that standard long-context adaptation can remain brittle: model accuracy depends strongly on the absolute placement of relevant evidence, exhibiting high positional variance even when controlling for task format and difficulty.
  We propose RoPE-Perturbed Self-Distillation, a training regularizer that improves positional robustness. The core idea is to form alternative "views" of the same training sequence by perturbing its RoPE indices -- effectively moving parts of the context to different positions -- and to train the model to produce consistent predictions across views via self-distillation. This encourages reliance on semantic signals instead of brittle position dependencies. Experiments on long-context adaptation of Llama-3-8B and Qwen-3-4B demonstrate consistent gains on long-context benchmarks, including up to 12.04% improvement on RULER-64K for Llama-3-8B and 2.71% on RULER-256K for Qwen-3-4B after SFT, alongside improved length extrapolation beyond the training context window.

### [97] [APEX-MEM: Agentic Semi-Structured Memory with Temporal Reasoning for Long-Term Conversational AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14362)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
