Abstract: Large language models still struggle with reliable long-term conversational memory: simply enlarging context windows or applying naive retrieval often introduces noise and destabilizes responses. We present APEX-MEM, a conversational memory system that combines three key innovations: (1) a property graph which uses domain-agnostic ontology to structure conversations as temporally grounded events in an entity-centric framework, (2) append-only storage that preserves the full temporal evolution of information, and (3) a multi-tool retrieval agent that understands and resolves conflicting or evolving information at query time, producing a compact and contextually relevant memory summary. This retrieval-time resolution preserves the full interaction history while suppressing irrelevant details. APEX-MEM achieves 88.88% accuracy on LOCOMO's Question Answering task and 86.2% on LongMemEval, outperforming state-of-the-art session-aware approaches and demonstrating that structured property graphs enable more temporally coherent long-term conversational reasoning.

### [98] [The Cost of Language: Centroid Erasure Exposes and Exploits Modal Competition in Multimodal Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14363)
*Akshay Paruchuri,Ishan Chatterjee,Henry Fuchs,Ehsan Adeli,Piotr Didyk*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出通过将每个标记替换为其最近的K-means质心（即中心点替换）来系统研究多模态语言模型在视觉感知任务中的表现不足问题。实验发现，移除文本中心点结构导致的准确率下降是移除视觉中心点结构的4倍，揭示了语言表示对视觉的普遍主导现象。作者进一步提出基于文本中心点擦除的对比解码方法，在多个任务上最高提升16.9%准确率，且该效果与训练方式相关：标准微调模型收益更大（平均+5.6%），而偏好优化模型收益较小（平均+1.5%）。结果表明，模态竞争具有结构性局部特征，可在推理阶段修正，且可作为未来多模态训练的诊断信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态语言模型在视觉感知任务中表现不佳，但其背后的原因尚不明确。本文旨在探究这种性能差距的结构根源，尤其是语言与视觉模态之间的依赖关系失衡问题。

Method: 提出中心点替换（centroid replacement）作为可控探针，通过移除文本或视觉模态的中心点结构，量化其对模型性能的影响；在此基础上设计文本中心点擦除的对比解码策略以恢复视觉推理能力。

Result: 移除文本中心点结构导致的准确率损失是视觉的4倍，表明语言模态在多模态模型中占据主导地位；通过对比解码干预，最大可提升16.9%准确率，且效果受训练方式影响显著。

Conclusion: 模态间的竞争具有结构性、局部化特征，可通过推理阶段干预纠正，且该现象可作为衡量和指导未来多模态训练的有效诊断信号。

Abstract: Multimodal language models systematically underperform on visual perception tasks, yet the structure underlying this failure remains poorly understood. We propose centroid replacement, collapsing each token to its nearest K-means centroid, as a controlled probe for modal dependence. Across seven models spanning three architecture families, erasing text centroid structure costs 4$\times$ more accuracy than erasing visual centroid structure, exposing a universal imbalance where language representations overshadow vision even on tasks that demand visual reasoning. We exploit this asymmetry through text centroid contrastive decoding, recovering up to +16.9% accuracy on individual tasks by contrastively decoding against a text-centroid-erased reference. This intervention varies meaningfully with training approaches: standard fine-tuned models show larger gains (+5.6% on average) than preference-optimized models (+1.5% on average). Our findings suggest that modal competition is structurally localized, correctable at inference time without retraining, and quantifiable as a diagnostic signal to guide future multimodal training.

### [99] [BiCon-Gate: Consistency-Gated De-colloquialisation for Dialogue Fact-Checking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14389)

TL;DR: 本文针对对话中自动事实核查的挑战，提出一种分阶段去口语化的方法，结合轻量级表面归一化与范围限定的指代消解，生成保守的重写候选。引入语义感知的一致性门控机制（BiCon-Gate），仅在上下文支持时选择重写候选，否则保留原始陈述。该方法提升了下游事实核查的稳定性，在DialFact基准上显著改善了证据检索与事实验证效果，尤其在SUPPORTS类别表现突出，优于包括基于解码器的单次大模型重写的竞争基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对话中的事实核查面临口语化语言频繁出现但研究不足的问题，现有方法难以有效处理非正式表达，导致事实核查不准确或不稳定。

Method: 采用分阶段去口语化策略，先进行轻量级表面归一化，再进行范围限定的指代消解；设计BiCon-Gate门控机制，依据对话上下文判断是否采纳重写候选，实现语义一致性控制。

Result: 在DialFact基准上，该方法在证据检索和事实验证任务中均取得提升，特别是在支持类（SUPPORTS）任务中表现尤为突出，优于多个先进基线模型，包括单次大模型重写方法。

Conclusion: 通过分阶段去口语化与语义感知门控机制，本方法有效提升了多轮对话中事实核查的准确性与稳定性，为应对口语化语言挑战提供了高效解决方案。

Abstract: Automated fact-checking in dialogue involves multi-turn conversations where colloquial language is frequent yet understudied. To address this gap, we propose a conservative rewrite candidate for each response claim via staged de-colloquialisation, combining lightweight surface normalisation with scoped in-claim coreference resolution. We then introduce BiCon-Gate, a semantics-aware consistency gate that selects the rewrite candidate only when it is semantically supported by the dialogue context, otherwise falling back to the original claim. This gated selection stabilises downstream fact-checking and yields gains in both evidence retrieval and fact verification. On the DialFact benchmark, our approach improves retrieval and verification, with particularly strong gains on SUPPORTS, and outperforms competitive baselines, including a decoder-based one-shot LLM rewrite that attempts to perform all de-colloquialisation steps in a single pass.

### [100] [Generating Concept Lexicalizations via Dictionary-Based Cross-Lingual Sense Projection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14397)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于英语有标注语料及其翻译，通过语义投影将英语同义词集（synsets）映射到目标语言对齐词元，并结合双语词典进行对齐与错误过滤，实现目标语言词素的意义生成。

Result: 在多语言上的实验表明，所提方法在保持高可解释性的同时显著提升了投影精度，优于已有方法及词典与大模型基线。

Conclusion: 该方法有效实现了跨语言词典资源的自动扩展，具有低资源需求、高精度和良好可解释性，未来将公开代码、文档及生成的词义资源。

Abstract: We study the task of automatically expanding WordNet-style lexical resources to new languages through sense generation. We generate senses by associating target-language lemmas with existing lexical concepts via semantic projection. Given a sense-tagged English corpus and its translation, our method projects English synsets onto aligned target-language tokens and assigns the corresponding lemmas to those synsets. To generate these alignments and ensure their quality, we augment a pre-trained base aligner with a bilingual dictionary, which is also used to filter out incorrect sense projections. We evaluate the method on multiple languages, comparing it to prior methods, as well as dictionary-based and large language model baselines. Results show that the proposed project-and-filter strategy improves precision while remaining interpretable and requiring few external resources. We plan to make our code, documentation, and generated sense inventories accessible.

</details>


### [101] [The Autocorrelation Blind Spot: Why 42% of Turn-Level Findings in LLM Conversation Analysis May Be Spurious](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14414)
*Ferdinand M. Schessl*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文系统分析了多轮人-大模型对话中66个轮次级指标的自相关结构，发现当前评估流程普遍忽略轮次间的非独立性，导致显著性估计严重膨胀。通过提出两阶段校正框架（结合Chelton有效自由度与对话级别块重采样），验证了校正后结果的可靠性，且仅42%的原显著关联在修正后仍显著。研究还发现不同指标类别受自相关影响程度差异大，部分类别甚至达到100%的误报率。作者提供设计原则、出版检查清单及开源代码，并指出近30篇顶会论文中仅有4篇提及时间依赖性，26篇未做任何校正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法在分析多轮对话时忽略了轮次间的自相关性，导致统计推断错误，显著性估计被严重高估，亟需一种能正确处理时间依赖性的校正方法。

Method: 采用系统性分析方法，对202个多轮对话中的11,639个轮对进行分析，识别66个轮次级指标的自相关模式；提出两阶段校正框架：第一阶段使用Chelton (1983)的有效自由度调整，第二阶段采用对话级别的块重采样进行稳健性检验；并通过预注册的保留数据集验证校正效果。

Result: 42%原本显著的关联在经过集群稳健校正后不再显著；不同指标类别受影响程度不一，记忆无关类平均影响14%，非记忆无关类平均影响33%，个别类别最高达100%；校正后模型复制率从30%提升至57%。

Conclusion: 当前大多数基于轮次级指标的评估方法因未考虑时间依赖性而存在严重的统计偏差。必须引入合适的校正机制以确保结果可信。本文提出的两阶段校正框架有效缓解了这一问题，并建议在相关研究中强制采用类似校正流程和透明报告标准。

Abstract: Turn-level metrics are widely used to evaluate properties of multi-turn human-LLM conversations, from safety and sycophancy to dialogue quality. However, consecutive turns within a conversation are not statistically independent -- a fact that virtually all current evaluation pipelines fail to correct for in their statistical inference. We systematically characterize the autocorrelation structure of 66 turn-level metrics across 202 multi-turn conversations (11,639 turn pairs, 5 German-speaking users, 4 LLM platforms) and demonstrate that naive pooled analysis produces severely inflated significance estimates: 42% of associations that appear significant under standard pooled testing fail to survive cluster-robust correction. The inflation varies substantially across categories rather than scaling linearly with autocorrelation: three memoryless families (embedding velocity, directional, differential) aggregate to 14%, while the seven non-memoryless families (thermo-cycle, frame distance, lexical/structural, rolling windows, cumulative, interaction, timestamp) aggregate to 33%, with individual category rates ranging from 0% to 100% depending on per-family effect size. We present a two-stage correction framework combining Chelton (1983) effective degrees of freedom with conversation-level block bootstrap, and validate it on a pre-registered hold-out split where cluster-robust metrics replicate at 57% versus 30% for pooled-only metrics. We provide concrete design principles, a publication checklist, and open-source code for the correction pipeline. A survey of ~30 recent papers at major NLP and AI venues that compute turn-level statistics in LLM evaluations finds that only 4 address temporal dependence at all, and 26 do not correct for it.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出HRM-LM模型，采用双速递归对结构：快模块每步执行局部精炼，慢模块每T步执行全局压缩；整个递归结构展开为M = N x T步，且参数共享。

Conclusion: 尽管递归结构可减少参数量，但其表征能力仍显著低于独立层堆叠，说明当前递归设计难以完全替代多层独立结构。

Abstract: We present an empirical study of whether hierarchically structured, shared-weight recurrence can match the representational quality of independent-layer stacking in a Transformer-based language model. HRM-LM replaces L independent Transformer layers with a two-speed recurrent pair: a Fast module operating at every step for local refinement, and a Slow module operating every T steps for global compression. This recurrent hierarchy is unrolled for M = N x T steps with shared parameters. The central and most robust finding, supported by a parameter-matched Universal Transformer ablation (UniTF, 1.2B) across five independent runs, is a sharp empirical gap between the two approaches.

Abstract: For humans, filler-gap dependencies require a shared representation across different syntactic constructions. Although causal analyses suggest this may also be true for LLMs (Boguraev et al., 2025), it is still unclear if such a representation also exists for language models trained on developmentally feasible quantities of data. We applied Distributed Alignment Search (DAS, Geiger et al. (2024)) to LMs trained on varying amounts of data from the BabyLM challenge (Warstadt et al., 2023), to evaluate whether representations of filler-gap dependencies transfer between wh-questions and topicalization, which greatly vary in terms of their input frequency. Our results suggest shared, yet item-sensitive mechanisms may develop with limited training data. More importantly, LMs still require far more data than humans to learn comparable generalizations, highlighting the need for language-specific biases in models of language acquisition.

### [104] [Psychological Steering of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14463)
*Leonardo Blas,Robin Jia,Emilio Ferrara*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种心理引导框架，通过语义校准的单位进行无界、流畅性约束的残差流注入，以优化大语言模型的心理特征控制。相较于传统基于未校准激活空间的搜索方法，该框架使用IPIP-NEO-120量表评估六种注入方法，发现均值差（MD）注入在14个LLM中的11个上优于现有基线P$^2$，提升达3.6%至16.4%；混合方法更优，在13个模型中超越两者，增益达5.6%至26.7%。研究还表明MD注入支持线性表示假设，具备可靠的线性控制能力，但其诱发的人格特质协方差模式偏离大二模型，揭示了模型表征与人类心理之间的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于残差流注入的心理控制方法受限于未校准的激活空间单位，搜索范围有限且难以找到最优干预条件。为实现更精准、可解释的心理特征调控，亟需一种语义校准、无界且受流畅性约束的新型注入框架。

Method: 提出一种心理引导框架，利用心理学工具（IPIP-NEO-120）校准残差流注入单位，进行无边界、流畅性约束的参数扫描。通过对比六种注入方法，包括均值差（MD）注入与人格提示（P$^2$），系统评估其在多模型上的表现。

Result: MD注入在11/14模型中优于P$^2$，提升3.6%至16.4%；混合方法在13/14模型中同时优于两者，增益分别达5.6%–21.9%和3.3%–26.7%。此外，MD注入表现出近似线性控制特性，符合线性表示假设，但其人格特质间协方差模式不符合大二模型，反映模型与真实心理结构存在差异。

Conclusion: 本研究确立了表示工程在开放生成场景下心理引导中的新前沿地位，证明了语义校准的残差流注入具有更强的可控性和有效性。尽管存在与人类心理结构的偏差，但该方法提供了可扩展、可解释的心理控制路径，为未来人机心理对齐研究提供新范式。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) emulate a consistent human-like behavior that can be shaped through activation-level interventions. This paradigm is converging on additive residual-stream injections, which rely on injection-strength sweeps to approximate optimal intervention settings. However, existing methods restrict the search space and sweep in uncalibrated activation-space units, potentially missing optimal intervention conditions. Thus, we introduce a psychological steering framework that performs unbounded, fluency-constrained sweeps in semantically calibrated units. Our method derives and calibrates residual-stream injections using psychological artifacts, and we use the IPIP-NEO-120, which measures the OCEAN personality model, to compare six injection methods. We find that mean-difference (MD) injections outperform Personality Prompting (P$^2$), an established baseline for OCEAN steering, in open-ended generation in 11 of 14 LLMs, with gains of 3.6\% to 16.4\%, overturning prior reports favoring prompting and positioning representation engineering as a new frontier in open-ended psychological steering. Further, we find that a hybrid of P$^2$ and MD injections outperforms both methods in 13 of 14 LLMs, with gains over P$^2$ ranging from 5.6\% to 21.9\% and from 3.3\% to 26.7\% over MD injections. Finally, we show that MD injections align with the Linear Representation Hypothesis and provide reliable, approximately linear control knobs for psychological steering. Nevertheless, they also induce OCEAN trait covariance patterns that depart from the Big Two model, suggesting a gap between learned representations and human psychology.

Abstract: Topic modeling seeks to uncover latent semantic structure in text corpora with minimal supervision. Neural approaches achieve strong performance but require extensive tuning and struggle with lifelong learning due to catastrophic forgetting and fixed capacity, while classical probabilistic models lack flexibility and adaptability to streaming data. We introduce \textsc{CobwebTM}, a low-parameter lifelong hierarchical topic model based on incremental probabilistic concept formation. This design enables systematic evaluation of whether detectors identify the origin of the surface text or the origin of the evaluative reasoning. We benchmark state-of-the-art LLM text detection methods on PeerPrism. While several methods achieve high accuracy on the standard binary task (human vs. fully synthetic), their predictions diverge sharply under hybrid regimes. In particular, when ideas originate from humans but the surface text is AI-generated, detectors frequently disagree and produce contradictory classifications. Accompanied by stylometric and semantic analyses, our results show that current detection methods conflate surface realization with intellectual contribution.
  Overall, we demonstrate that LLM detection in peer review cannot be reduced to a binary attribution problem. Instead, authorship must be modeled as a multidimensional construct spanning semantic reasoning and stylistic realization. PeerPrism is the first benchmark evaluating human-AI collaboration in these settings. We release all code, data, prompts, and evaluation scripts to facilitate reproducible research at https://github.com/Reviewerly-Inc/PeerPrism.

### [107] [Mechanistic Decoding of Cognitive Constructs in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14593)

Main category: cs.CL

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate increasingly sophisticated affective capabilities, the internal mechanisms by which they process complex emotions remain unclear. Existing interpretability approaches often treat models as black boxes or focus on coarse-grained basic emotions, leaving the cognitive structure of more complex affective states underexplored. To bridge this gap, we propose a Cognitive Reverse-Engineering framework based on Representation Engineering (RepE) to analyze social-comparison jealousy. By combining appraisal theory with subspace orthogonalization, regression-based weighting, and bidirectional causal steering, we isolate and quantify two psychological antecedents of jealousy, Superiority of Comparison Person and Domain Self-Definitional Relevance, and examine their causal effects on model judgments. Experiments on eight LLMs from the Llama, Qwen, and Gemma families suggest that models natively encode jealousy as a structured linear combination of these constituent factors. Their internal representations are broadly consistent with the human psychological construct, treating Superiority as the foundational trigger and Relevance as the ultimate intensity multiplier. Our framework also demonstrates that toxic emotional states can be mechanically detected and surgically suppressed, suggesting a possible route toward representational monitoring and intervention for AI safety in multi-agent environments.

*Joshua Tint*

TL;DR: 本文指出，近年来自然语言处理（NLP）领域在多样性方面的进展主要集中于公平性相关方向，而这一现象源于一系列激励机制、偏见与障碍，导致边缘化研究者难以在非公平性领域参与或被迫转向公平性研究。作者通过分析不同子领域中NLP研究人员的背景数据，支持了多项建议，强调需打破强化不平等的反馈循环，并解决地理与语言壁垒以促进整个NLP领域的包容性与公平性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前NLP领域多样性进展过度集中于公平性议题，忽视了其他重要方向，这种不平衡可能源于系统性障碍和激励机制，不利于边缘化群体在多元领域的发展。

Method: 基于对NLP研究人员按子领域划分的统计数据进行分析，考察其人口构成差异，识别出结构性不平等的表现与成因。

Result: 研究发现，非公平性子领域中边缘化群体代表性显著偏低，且存在地理与语言壁垒限制参与；反馈循环加剧了现有不平等。

Conclusion: 为实现全领域的包容与公平，必须打破强化不平等的反馈机制，消除地理与语言障碍，并鼓励多元化研究方向的发展。

Abstract: This position paper argues that recent progress with diversity in NLP is disproportionately concentrated on a small number of areas surrounding fairness. We further argue that this is the result of a number of incentives, biases, and barriers which come together to disenfranchise marginalized researchers in non-fairness fields, or to move them into fairness-related fields. We substantiate our claims with an investigation into the demographics of NLP researchers by subfield, using our research to support a number of recommendations for ensuring that all areas within NLP can become more inclusive and equitable. In particular, we highlight the importance of breaking down feedback loops that reinforce disparities, and the need to address geographical and linguistic barriers that hinder participation in NLP research.

### [109] [CausalDetox: Causal Head Selection and Intervention for Language Model Detoxification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14602)
*Yian Wang,Yuen Chen,Agam Goyal,Hari Sundaram*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CAUSALDETOX 是一种用于识别和干预导致生成有毒内容的特定注意力头的框架，利用 PNS 方法确定必要且充分的注意力头，并通过推理时动态干预和基于 PNS 的微调两种策略实现去毒化。引入 PARATOX 基准用于可控反事实评估，实验表明其在毒性减少上优于基线最多 5.34%，同时保持语言流畅性，并实现 7 倍的头选择速度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型常生成有毒内容，现有缓解策略要么降低生成质量，要么需要昂贵的人工标注。亟需一种高效、精准且不损害生成质量的去毒方法。

Method: 使用概率必要性与充分性（PNS）识别对毒性生成必要且充分的注意力头；采用两种互补策略：局部推理时干预（构建上下文感知的动态引导向量）和 PNS 引导微调（永久消除毒性表征）；引入 PARATOX 基准进行可控反事实评估。

Result: 在 ToxiGen、ImplicitHate 和 ParaDetox 数据集上，CAUSALDETOX 比基线最多减少 5.34% 的毒性，同时保持语言流畅性，并实现 7 倍于传统方法的注意力头选择速度。

Conclusion: CAUSALDETOX 提供了一种高效、精准且可扩展的去毒框架，能够有效减少大模型中的毒性输出，同时维持生成质量，为安全部署提供新路径。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) frequently generate toxic content, posing significant risks for safe deployment. Current mitigation strategies often degrade generation quality or require costly human annotation. We propose CAUSALDETOX, a framework that identifies and intervenes on the specific attention heads causally responsible for toxic generation. Using the Probability of Necessity and Sufficiency (PNS), we isolate a minimal set of heads that are necessary and sufficient for toxicity. We utilize these components via two complementary strategies: (1) Local Inference-Time Intervention, which constructs dynamic, input-specific steering vectors for context-aware detoxification, and (2) PNS-Guided Fine-Tuning, which permanently unlearns toxic representations. We also introduce PARATOX, a novel benchmark of aligned toxic/non-toxic sentence pairs enabling controlled counterfactual evaluation. Experiments on ToxiGen, ImplicitHate, and ParaDetox show that CAUSALDETOX achieves up to 5.34% greater toxicity reduction compared to baselines while preserving linguistic fluency, and offers a 7x speedup in head selection.

### [110] [Retrieve, Then Classify: Corpus-Grounded Automation of Clinical Value Set Authoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14616)
*Sumit Mukherjee,Juan Shu,Nairwita Mazumder,Tate Kernell,Celena Wheeler,Shannon Hastings,Chris Sidey-Gibbons*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出RASC（检索增强的集合补全）方法，通过从已有的价值集库中检索最相似的K个值集作为候选池，再使用分类器筛选有效代码，显著降低输出空间复杂度。在11,803个公开的VSAC值集上构建首个大规模基准数据集，实验表明该方法在AUROC（0.852）和值集级F1（0.298）上优于MLP和零样本GPT-4o，且能有效减少无关候选数量。性能提升在不同模型类型中均一致，验证了方法的普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床价值集编写是临床质量测量与表型分析中的常见瓶颈。直接用大语言模型生成代码存在词汇表庞大、版本控制复杂及预训练期间记忆不充分的问题，亟需更高效精准的方法。

Method: RASC方法包含两阶段：首先从结构化语料库中检索与目标概念最相似的K个现有值集形成候选池；然后利用分类器对候选池中的每个代码进行评估，筛选出符合要求的代码。

Result: RASC在跨编码器微调后达到AUROC 0.852，值集级F1为0.298，显著优于基础MLP（AUROC 0.799，F1 0.250）和零样本GPT-4o（F1 0.105）。同时将每条真实正例对应的无关候选数从12.3降至约3.2和4.4。性能优势随值集规模增加而扩大，且在多种分类器中保持一致。

Conclusion: RASC通过检索-选择机制有效缩小输出空间，显著提升临床价值集生成的准确性与效率，具备良好的泛化能力，为临床知识自动化提供有力支持。

Abstract: Clinical value set authoring -- the task of identifying all codes in a standardized vocabulary that define a clinical concept -- is a recurring bottleneck in clinical quality measurement and phenotyping. A natural approach is to prompt a large language model (LLM) to generate the required codes directly, but structured clinical vocabularies are large, version-controlled, and not reliably memorized during pretraining. We propose Retrieval-Augmented Set Completion (RASC): retrieve the $K$ most similar existing value sets from a curated corpus to form a candidate pool, then apply a classifier to each candidate code. Theoretically, retrieve-and-select can reduce statistical complexity by shrinking the effective output space from the full vocabulary to a much smaller retrieved candidate pool. We demonstrate the utility of RASC on 11,803 publicly available VSAC value sets, constructing the first large-scale benchmark for this task. A cross-encoder fine-tuned on SAPBert achieves AUROC~0.852 and value-set-level F1~0.298, outperforming a simpler three-layer Multilayer Perceptron (AUROC~0.799, F1~0.250) and both reduce the number of irrelevant candidates per true positive from 12.3 (retrieval-only) to approximately 3.2 and 4.4 respectively. Zero-shot GPT-4o achieves value-set-level F1~0.105, with 48.6\% of returned codes absent from VSAC entirely. This performance gap widens with increasing value set size, consistent with RASC's theoretical advantage. We observe similar performance gains across two other classifier model types, namely a cross-encoder initialized from pre-trained SAPBert and a LightGBM model, demonstrating that RASC's benefits extend beyond a single model class. The code to download and create the benchmark dataset, as well as the model training code is available at: \href{https://github.com/mukhes3/RASC}{https://github.com/mukhes3/RASC}.

</details>


### [111] [StoryCoder: Narrative Reformulation for Structured Reasoning in LLM Code Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14631)
*Geonhui Jang,Dongyoon Han,YoungJoon Yoo*

TL;DR: StoryCoder提出一种叙事重构框架，将代码生成问题转化为连贯的自然语言叙述，包含任务概述、约束和示例测试用例，提升模型推理与规划能力。在11个模型上实验显示，零样本pass@10平均提升18.7%。分析表明，该方法引导模型选择正确算法策略，减少实现错误，促进模块化代码结构，且效果依赖于叙事连贯性与类型匹配。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法虽增强推理步骤或注入思维结构，但未有效整合零散的问题条件。受人类组织碎片信息为连贯解释的启发，需更系统地重构问题表示以提升代码生成质量。

Method: 设计叙事重构框架StoryCoder，将原始问题转化为包含任务概述、约束和示例测试用例的自然语言叙述，依据选定算法与代码类型进行结构化表达。

Result: 在HumanEval、LiveCodeBench和CodeForces上，11个模型的零样本pass@10平均提升18.7%；分析显示模型更倾向正确算法策略，实现错误减少，代码结构更模块化。

Conclusion: 结构化的问题表示对代码生成至关重要，其效果不依赖模型规模或架构，叙事连贯性与类型对齐是关键因素。代码已开源。

Abstract: Effective code generation requires both model capability and a problem representation that carefully structures how models reason and plan. Existing approaches augment reasoning steps or inject specific structure into how models think, but leave scattered problem conditions unchanged. Inspired by the way humans organize fragmented information into coherent explanations, we propose StoryCoder, a narrative reformulation framework that transforms code generation questions into coherent natural language narratives, providing richer contextual structure than simple rephrasings. Each narrative consists of three components: a task overview, constraints, and example test cases, guided by the selected algorithm and genre. Experiments across 11 models on HumanEval, LiveCodeBench, and CodeForces demonstrate consistent improvements, with an average gain of 18.7% in zero-shot pass@10. Beyond accuracy, our analyses reveal that narrative reformulation guides models toward correct algorithmic strategies, reduces implementation errors, and induces a more modular code structure. The analyses further show that these benefits depend on narrative coherence and genre alignment, suggesting that structured problem representation is important for code generation regardless of model scale or architecture. Our code is available at https://github.com/gu-ni/StoryCoder.

### [112] [Pushing the Boundaries of Multiple Choice Evaluation to One Hundred Options](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14634)
*Nahyun Lee,Guijin Son*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种大规模选项评估协议，将候选集扩展至100个选项，以降低随机性能的影响，并在韩语拼写错误检测任务中验证其有效性。通过固定目标与重复重采样，获得稳定评估结果，区分内容相关错误与位置偏差。实验表明，低选项设置下的高性能可能夸大模型能力，而在高干扰密度下这些优势减弱，暴露出传统基准未揭示的缺陷。识别出两种失败模式：语义混淆和不确定性下对早期选项的位置偏好。控制填充和长度匹配测试表明，主要瓶颈是候选排序而非上下文长度。研究支持大规模选项评估作为压力测试模型可靠性的通用框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于多项选择的评估在低选项数量下容易被捷径策略误导，导致模型真实能力被高估，因此需要更严格的评估方法来揭示模型在高干扰密度下的真实表现。

Method: 提出大规模选项评估协议，将候选集扩大至100个选项；在韩语拼写错误检测任务中应用该框架，通过固定目标、重复重采样与洗牌，分离内容驱动错误与位置偏差；进行填充控制与长度匹配测试，分析上下文长度与候选排序的影响。

Result: 低选项设置下的强表现常在高选项设置下减弱，暴露出模型的真实局限性；识别出语义混淆和早期选项位置偏好两种失败模式；候选排序是主要瓶颈，而非上下文长度。

Conclusion: 大规模选项评估可有效压力测试模型在极端干扰密度下的可靠性，是超越传统低选项基准的更优评估范式。

Abstract: Multiple choice evaluation is widely used for benchmarking large language models, yet near ceiling accuracy in low option settings can be sustained by shortcut strategies that obscure true competence. Therefore, we propose a massive option evaluation protocol that scales the candidate set to one hundred options and sharply reduces the impact of chance performance. We apply this framework to a Korean orthography error detection task where models must pick the single incorrect sentence from a large candidate set. With fixed targets and repeated resampling and shuffling, we obtain stable estimates while separating content driven failures from positional artifacts. Across experiments, results indicate that strong performance in low option settings can overstate model competence. This apparent advantage often weakens under dense interference at high $N$, revealing gaps that conventional benchmarks tend to obscure. We identify two failure modes, semantic confusion and position bias toward early options under uncertainty. To isolate the effect of context length, we run padding controlled and length matched tests, which suggest that the main bottleneck is candidate ranking rather than context length. Together, these findings support massive option evaluation as a general framework for stress testing model reliability under extreme distractor density, beyond what low option benchmarks can reveal.

Detecting such misleading narratives is inherently challenging, particularly in real-world scenarios where external evidence or supplementary references for cross-verification are strictly unavailable. This paper presents our winning methodology for the "Reference-Free Financial Misinformation Detection" shared task. Built upon the recently proposed RFC-BENCH framework (Jiang et al. 2026), this task challenges models to determine the veracity of financial claims by relying solely on internal semantic understanding and contextual consistency, rather than external fact-checking. To address this formidable evaluation setup, we propose a comprehensive framework that capitalizes on the reasoning capabilities of state-of-the-art Large Language Models (LLMs). Our approach systematically integrates in-context learning, specifically zero-shot and few-shot prompting strategies, with Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning (PEFT) via Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) to optimally align the models with the subtle linguistic cues of financial manipulation. Our proposed system demonstrated superior efficacy, successfully securing the first-place ranking on both official leaderboards. Specifically, we achieved an accuracy of 95.4% on the public test set and 96.3% on the private test set, highlighting the robustness of our method and contributing to the acceleration of context-aware misinformation detection in financial Natural Language Processing. Our models (14B and 32B) are available at https://huggingface.co/KaiNKaiho.

### [114] [CURaTE: Continual Unlearning in Real Time with Ensured Preservation of LLM Knowledge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14644)
*Seyun Bae,Seokhan Lee,Eunho Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CURaTE 是一种实时持续遗忘方法，通过训练句子嵌入模型来快速判断输入是否匹配遗忘请求，从而决定是否回应。该方法无需修改模型参数，实现了高效遗忘与近乎完美的知识保留，支持无限次更新且可实时处理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有遗忘方法无法持续、即时地处理敏感信息，导致知识泄露风险累积和性能下降。需要一种能实时、连续地遗忘特定知识而不损害模型整体能力的方法。

Method: 训练一个句子嵌入模型，用于构建清晰的决策边界，判断输入是否匹配已知的遗忘请求；根据相似度决定是否拒绝回答，不修改语言模型参数。

Result: CURaTE 在遗忘效果上优于现有方法，且在多次更新后仍保持接近完美的知识保留，唯一支持实时持续遗忘。

Abstract: The inability to filter out in advance all potentially problematic data from the pre-training of large language models has given rise to the need for methods for unlearning specific pieces of knowledge after training. Existing techniques overlook the need for continuous and immediate action, causing them to suffer from degraded utility as updates accumulate and protracted exposure of sensitive information. To address these issues, we propose Continual Unlearning in Real Time with Ensured Preservation of LLM Knowledge (CURaTE). Our method begins by training a sentence embedding model on a dataset designed to enable the formation of sharp decision boundaries for determining whether a given input prompt corresponds to any stored forget requests. The similarity of a given input to the forget requests is then used to determine whether to answer or return a refusal response. We show that even with such a simple approach, not only does CURaTE achieve more effective forgetting than existing methods, but by avoiding modification of the language model parameters, it also maintains near perfect knowledge preservation over any number of updates and is the only method capable of continual unlearning in real-time.

### [115] [CURA: Clinical Uncertainty Risk Alignment for Language Model-Based Risk Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14651)
*Sizhe Wang,Ziqi Xu,Claire Najjuuko,Charles Alba,Chenyang Lu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Clinical Uncertainty Risk Alignment (CURA)框架，通过联合校准个体错误概率与群体层面的不确定性，提升临床语言模型在风险预测中的不确定性估计可靠性。CURA首先微调领域特定的临床语言模型以获得任务适配的患者嵌入，再通过双层不确定性目标对多头分类器进行不确定性微调：个体级校准项使预测不确定性与个体出错概率对齐，群体感知正则项则将风险估计拉向嵌入空间局部邻域内的事件率，并加强对决策边界附近模糊群体的权重。该正则项可解释为基于邻域信息的软标签交叉熵损失，提供了一种标签平滑视角。在MIMIC-IV数据集上的大量实验表明，CURA在不显著牺牲判别能力的前提下，持续改善校准性能，减少过度自信的误判，提升下游临床决策支持的可信度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床语言模型在自由文本笔记中用于风险预测时，其不确定性估计常存在校准不足、临床不可靠的问题。现有方法缺乏对个体错误可能性和群体层面模糊性的联合建模，导致预测结果虽有置信度但实际可信度不足。因此需要一种能同时对个体与群体不确定性进行有效校准的方法，以增强临床决策支持系统的可信赖性。

Method: CURA框架包含两阶段设计：1）使用领域特定临床语言模型微调生成任务适配的患者嵌入；2）通过双层不确定性目标对多头分类器进行不确定性微调，包括：(a) 个体级校准项，使预测不确定性与个体出错概率一致；(b) 群体感知正则项，将风险估计拉向嵌入空间局部邻域的事件率，并强化对靠近决策边界的模糊群体的惩罚。该正则项可被形式化为带邻域软标签的交叉熵损失，实现标签平滑式校准。

Result: 在MIMIC-IV多个临床风险预测任务上，CURA显著提升了校准指标（如ECE），同时保持了良好的判别能力（如AUROC）。分析显示，CURA有效减少了模型对高风险患者的过度自信误判，提高了不确定性估计的临床可信度，尤其在边缘病例和模糊群体中表现更稳健。

Conclusion: CURA通过融合个体误差对齐与群体模糊性感知，实现了临床语言模型风险预测中不确定性估计的精准校准。该方法不仅提升了模型的可靠性，也为构建可信赖的临床决策支持系统提供了新范式。

Abstract: Clinical language models (LMs) are increasingly applied to support clinical risk prediction from free-text notes, yet their uncertainty estimates often remain poorly calibrated and clinically unreliable. In this work, we propose Clinical Uncertainty Risk Alignment (CURA), a framework that aligns clinical LM-based risk estimates and uncertainty with both individual error likelihoods and cohort-level ambiguities. CURA first fine-tunes domain-specific clinical LMs to obtain task-adapted patient embeddings, and then performs uncertainty fine-tuning of a multi-head classifier using a bi-level uncertainty objective. Specifically, an individual-level calibration term aligns predictive uncertainty with each patient's likelihood of error, while a cohort-aware regularizer pulls risk estimates toward event rates in their local neighborhoods in the embedding space and places extra weight on ambiguous cohorts near the decision boundary. We further show that this cohort-aware term can be interpreted as a cross-entropy loss with neighborhood-informed soft labels, providing a label-smoothing view of our method. Extensive experiments on MIMIC-IV clinical risk prediction tasks across various clinical LMs show that CURA consistently improves calibration metrics without substantially compromising discrimination. Further analysis illustrates that CURA reduces overconfident false reassurance and yields more trustworthy uncertainty estimates for downstream clinical decision support.

</details>


### [116] [SPAGBias: Uncovering and Tracing Structured Spatial Gender Bias in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14672)
*Binxian Su,Haoye Lou,Shucheng Zhu,Weikang Wang,Ying Liu,Dong Yu,Pengyuan Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出SPAGBias框架，系统评估大语言模型（LLMs）中的空间性别偏见。通过62种城市微观空间分类、提示库及三重诊断层（显式、概率性、建构性分析），发现模型存在超越公共-私人二分法的细微性别空间关联。生成故事显示情感、用词与社会角色共同塑造‘空间性别叙事’，且偏见在预训练、指令微调和奖励建模中被强化，远超现实分布。下游实验表明此类偏见导致规范性和描述性应用中的具体失败。研究将社会理论与计算分析结合，揭示LLM如何通过语言编码社会性别认知。

Method: 提出SPAGBias框架，包含62种城市微观空间的分类体系、提示库，以及三种诊断层次：显式（强制选择重采样）、概率性（标记级不对称）和建构性（语义与叙事角色分析）。通过多轮测试与追踪实验，分析不同模型规模、提示设计、温度参数对偏见表达的影响。

Result: 发现模型中存在结构化的性别-空间关联，超出传统的公共-私人划分，形成细微的微观映射；故事生成揭示情绪、语言和角色共同构建空间性别叙事；偏见在模型训练全流程中被嵌入并增强，显著高于真实世界分布；下游任务中表现出明显的应用失败。

Conclusion: 本研究首次系统揭示了大语言模型在空间维度上的性别偏见，证明其不仅反映社会现实，更可能加剧不平等。研究连接社会学理论与计算分析，为未来开发公平、可解释的智能城市系统提供重要依据。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are being increasingly used in urban planning, but since gendered space theory highlights how gender hierarchies are embedded in spatial organization, there is concern that LLMs may reproduce or amplify such biases. We introduce SPAGBias - the first systematic framework to evaluate spatial gender bias in LLMs. It combines a taxonomy of 62 urban micro-spaces, a prompt library, and three diagnostic layers: explicit (forced-choice resampling), probabilistic (token-level asymmetry), and constructional (semantic and narrative role analysis). Testing six representative models, we identify structured gender-space associations that go beyond the public-private divide, forming nuanced micro-level mappings. Story generation reveals how emotion, wording, and social roles jointly shape "spatial gender narratives". We also examine how prompt design, temperature, and model scale influence bias expression. Tracing experiments indicate that these patterns are embedded and reinforced across the model pipeline (pre-training, instruction tuning, and reward modeling), with model associations found to substantially exceed real-world distributions. Downstream experiments further reveal that such biases produce concrete failures in both normative and descriptive application settings. This work connects sociological theory with computational analysis, extending bias research into the spatial domain and uncovering how LLMs encode social gender cognition through language.

### [117] [Which bird does not have wings: Negative-constrained KGQA with Schema-guided Semantic Matching and Self-directed Refinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14749)
*Midan Shim,Seokju Hwang,Kaehyun Um,Kyong-Ho Lee*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出新的知识图谱问答任务NEST-KGQA，专注于包含至少一个否定约束的问题，并构建了相应的数据集NestKGQA。为清晰表达否定逻辑，设计了Python格式的逻辑形式PyLF。针对多约束问题的语义复杂性，提出CUCKOO框架，通过约束感知的逻辑形式生成与模式引导的语义匹配，仅在执行失败时进行自导向优化，提升鲁棒性与效率。实验表明，CUCKOO在少样本设置下优于现有基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有知识图谱问答（KGQA）方法主要关注正向和计算类约束，忽视了现实问题中频繁出现的否定约束，导致模型在处理包含否定条件的问题时表现不佳。因此需要新的任务、数据集和方法来解决这一缺陷。

Method: 提出NEST-KGQA任务和NestKGQA数据集；设计可读性强且能清晰表达否定的Python格式逻辑形式PyLF；开发CUCKOO框架，包括约束感知的逻辑形式生成、模式引导的语义匹配，以及仅在结果为空时触发的自导向精炼机制。

Result: CUCKOO在常规KGQA和NEST-KGQA基准上均显著优于现有基线方法，尤其在少样本场景下表现突出，证明其对多约束及否定性问题的有效处理能力。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入否定约束驱动的新任务与相应技术体系，有效提升了大语言模型在复杂语义约束下的问答准确性与可靠性，为构建更忠实、更鲁棒的KGQA系统提供了新思路。

Abstract: Large language models still struggle with faithfulness and hallucinations despite their remarkable reasoning abilities. In Knowledge Graph Question Answering (KGQA), semantic parsing-based approaches address the limitations by understanding constraints in a user's question and converting them into a logical form to execute on a knowledge graph. However, existing KGQA benchmarks and methods are biased toward positive and calculation constraints. Negative constraints are neglected, although they frequently appear in real-world questions. In this paper, we introduce a new task, NEgative-conSTrained (NEST) KGQA, where each question contains at least one negative constraint, and a corresponding dataset, NestKGQA. We also design PyLF, a Python-formatted logical form, since existing logical forms are hardly suitable to express negation clearly while maintaining readability. Furthermore, NEST questions naturally contain multiple constraints. To mitigate their semantic complexity, we present a novel framework named CUCKOO, specialized to multiple-constrained questions and ensuring semantic executability. CUCKOO first generates a constraint-aware logical form draft and performs schema-guided semantic matching. It then selectively applies self-directed refinement only when executing improper logical forms yields an empty result, reducing cost while improving robustness. Experimental results demonstrate that CUCKOO consistently outperforms baselines on both conventional KGQA and NEST-KGQA benchmarks under few-shot settings.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在模型遗忘与性能保留之间存在难以调和的权衡，需要一种能够优先保障保留能力的同时有效实现遗忘的新范式。

Abstract: Machine unlearning for large language models (LLMs) aims to remove targeted knowledge while preserving general capability. In this paper, we recast LLM unlearning as an asymmetric two-task problem: retention is the primary objective and forgetting is an auxiliary. From this perspective, we propose a retention-prioritized gradient synthesis framework that decouples task-specific gradient extraction from conflict-aware combination. Instantiating the framework, we adapt established PCGrad to resolve gradient conflicts, and introduce SAGO, a novel retention-prioritized gradient synthesis method. Theoretically, both variants ensure non-negative cosine similarity with the retain gradient, while SAGO achieves strictly tighter alignment through constructive sign-constrained synthesis. Empirically, on WMDP Bio/Cyber and RWKU benchmarks, SAGO consistently pushes the Pareto frontier: e.g., on WMDP Bio (SimNPO+GD), recovery of target model MMLU performance progresses from 44.6% (naive) to 94.0% (+PCGrad) and further to 96.0% (+SAGO), while maintaining comparable forgetting strength. Our results show that re-shaping gradient geometry, rather than re-balancing losses, is the key to mitigating unlearning-retention trade-offs.

### [121] [Exploring and Testing Skill-Based Behavioral Profile Annotation: Human Operability and LLM Feasibility under Schema-Guided Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14843)
*Yufeng Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文将行为特征（BP）标注视为一组可分离的标注技能，而非单一任务。基于3,134个中文隐喻性颜色词派生语料和14维BP标注框架，构建了以技能文件驱动的标注流程，通过两轮人工标注验证，将标注技能分为可直接操作、可通过聚焦重标注恢复、结构不明确三类。评估GPT-5.4及三个开源模型发现：5项技能可直接执行，4项可恢复，5项仍结构不明确；GPT-5.4在保留技能上表现可靠（准确率0.678，kappa=0.665，加权F1=0.695），但其能力具有选择性而非全局性。人类与GPT在技能层面难度高度一致（r=0.881），但在实例和词汇层面几乎无相关性，呈现‘共享分类体系，独立执行’特征。对比表明，GPT更应被视为独立的第三方标注声音，而非人类替代者。开源模型失败主要源于从标注框架到技能执行的转化问题。研究建议自动标注评估应聚焦技能可行性，而非整体任务自动化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统行为特征（BP）标注难以自动化，因其需同时处理多个语言维度。现有方法常将整个标注视为单一任务，忽略了其内部技能的异质性。本文旨在从技能分解视角重新审视自动化标注的可行性，探索大模型在复杂标注任务中的真实作用，避免过度泛化其能力。

Method: 采用3,134条中文隐喻性颜色词派生语料，结合14维行为特征标注框架，构建基于技能文件驱动的标注系统。通过两轮人工标注验证，对每项标注技能进行分类（可直接操作、可恢复、结构不明确）。随后在相同设置下评估GPT-5.4与三个本地部署开源模型的表现，分析其在不同技能上的执行效果，并比较人类与模型间的难度分布与一致性。

Result: 共识别出14项标注技能：5项可直接操作，4项可通过聚焦重标注恢复，5项结构不明确。GPT-5.4在可执行技能上表现良好（准确率0.678，kappa=0.665，加权F1=0.695），但能力具有选择性。人类与GPT在技能层面难度高度一致（r=0.881），但在实例（r=0.016）和词汇层面（r=-0.142）几乎无关，体现‘共享分类体系，独立执行’模式。模型表现差异主要源于从标注框架到具体技能的映射问题，尤其是开源模型。

Conclusion: 自动标注不应以任务整体自动化为目标，而应以技能层面的可行性为评估标准。大模型如GPT-5.4并非人类的直接替代品，而是具备独特标注逻辑的独立技能执行者。未来工作应聚焦于技能建模与框架—技能映射机制优化，以提升自动标注系统的可靠性与可解释性。

Abstract: Behavioral Profile (BP) annotation is difficult to automate because it requires simultaneous coding across multiple linguistic dimensions. We treat BP annotation as a bundle of annotation skills rather than a single task and evaluate LLM-assisted BP annotation from this perspective. Using 3,134 concordance lines of 30 Chinese metaphorical color-term derivatives and a 14-feature BP schema, we implement a skill-file-driven pipeline in which each feature is externally defined through schema files, decision rules, and examples. Two human annotators completed a two-round schema-only protocol on a 300-instance validation subset, enabling BP skills to be classified as directly operable, recoverable under focused re-annotation, or structurally underspecified. GPT-5.4 and three locally deployable open-source models were then evaluated under the same setup. Results show that BP annotation is highly heterogeneous at the skill level: 5 skills are directly operable, 4 are recoverable after focused re-annotation, and 5 remain structurally underspecified. GPT-5.4 executes the retained skills with substantial reliability (accuracy = 0.678, \k{appa} = 0.665, weighted F1 = 0.695), but this feasibility is selective rather than global. Human and GPT difficulty profiles are strongly aligned at the skill level (r = 0.881), but not at the instance level (r = 0.016) or lexical-item level (r = -0.142), a pattern we describe as shared taxonomy, independent execution. Pairwise agreement further suggests that GPT is better understood as an independent third skill voice than as a direct human substitute. Open-source failures are concentrated in schema-to-skill execution problems. These findings suggest that automatic annotation should be evaluated in terms of skill feasibility rather than task-level automation.

### [122] [Segment-Level Coherence for Robust Harmful Intent Probing in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14865)
*Xuanli He,Bilgehan Sel,Faizan Ali,Jenny Bao,Hoagy Cunningham,Jerry Wei*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的流式探测方法，通过要求多个证据标记一致支持预测，而非依赖单一高分标记，以提升对高风险CBRN内容的检测鲁棒性。在固定1%误报率下，真阳性率相对强基线提升35.55%，且在接近饱和的基线性能（AUROC=97.40%）基础上仍有显著增益。此外，探测注意力或MLP激活优于残差流特征；即使面对字符级加密的对抗微调攻击，该方法仍可“即插即用”实现超过98.85%的AUROC。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有流式探测方法易因敏感词出现在良性上下文中产生误报，核心问题在于过度依赖少数高分标记，缺乏对上下文整体信号的整合。

Method: 提出一种基于多证据标记一致性的流式探测目标，强调聚合信号而非单个标记异常，同时比较不同模型层（注意力、MLP、残差流）的探测效果，并验证其在对抗性编码攻击下的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 通过引入多证据一致性机制，新方法显著提升了对高风险内容的实时检测准确性与鲁棒性，且具备良好的泛化能力，适用于复杂对抗场景。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly exposed to adaptive jailbreaking, particularly in high-stakes Chemical, Biological, Radiological, and Nuclear (CBRN) domains. Although streaming probes enable real-time monitoring, they still make systematic errors. We identify a core issue: existing methods often rely on a few high-scoring tokens, leading to false alarms when sensitive CBRN terms appear in benign contexts. To address this, we introduce a streaming probing objective that requires multiple evidence tokens to consistently support a prediction, rather than relying on isolated spikes. This encourages more robust detection based on aggregated signals instead of single-token cues. At a fixed 1% false-positive rate, our method improves the true-positive rate by 35.55% relative to strong streaming baselines. We further observe substantial gains in AUROC, even when starting from near-saturated baseline performance (AUROC = 97.40%). We also show that probing Attention or MLP activations consistently outperforms residual-stream features. Finally, even when adversarial fine-tuning enables novel character-level ciphers, harmful intent remains detectable: probes developed for the base LLMs can be applied ``plug-and-play'' to these obfuscated attacks, achieving an AUROC of over 98.85%.

### [123] [Reasoning Dynamics and the Limits of Monitoring Modality Reliance in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14888)
*Danae Sánchez Villegas,Samuel Lewis-Lim,Nikolaos Aletras,Desmond Elliott*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究分析了18个视觉语言模型（VLMs）在推理过程中的动态，发现模型存在回答惯性，即早期预测被强化而非修正。尽管推理训练模型表现出更强的纠错能力，但其效果依赖于模态条件。即使视觉证据充分，模型仍易受误导性文本线索影响，且这种影响在链式思维（CoT）中可检测性因模型而异。推理训练模型更明确提及线索，但其流畅的推理过程可能掩盖对文本的依赖；而指令微调模型提及较少，但较短的推理轨迹暴露与视觉输入的不一致。总体表明，CoT仅部分揭示多模态决策机制，对系统透明性和安全性具有重要启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解视觉语言模型（VLMs）如何整合视觉与文本信息进行推理，揭示其内在推理动态，以提升多模态系统的透明度与安全性。

Method: 通过追踪链式思维（CoT）中的置信度变化，评估推理步骤的纠正效应，并使用受控干预（如误导性文本线索）测试模型对不同模态的依赖程度，比较不同模型家族和训练方式的表现。

Result: 模型普遍存在回答惯性；推理训练模型纠错能力更强但依赖模态条件；文本线索即使在视觉证据充足时仍具影响力，且其可检测性因模型而异；推理训练模型更显式引用线索但可能伪装为视觉驱动，指令微调模型则通过简短推理暴露不一致。

Conclusion: 链式思维（CoT）仅提供多模态决策过程的部分视图，无法全面反映各模态的实际作用，提示需改进对多模态系统推理机制的理解与评估方法，以增强其透明性与安全性。

Abstract: Recent advances in vision language models (VLMs) offer reasoning capabilities, yet how these unfold and integrate visual and textual information remains unclear. We analyze reasoning dynamics in 18 VLMs covering instruction-tuned and reasoning-trained models from two different model families. We track confidence over Chain-of-Thought (CoT), measure the corrective effect of reasoning, and evaluate the contribution of intermediate reasoning steps. We find that models are prone to answer inertia, in which early commitments to a prediction are reinforced, rather than revised during reasoning steps. While reasoning-trained models show stronger corrective behavior, their gains depend on modality conditions, from text-dominant to vision-only settings. Using controlled interventions with misleading textual cues, we show that models are consistently influenced by these cues even when visual evidence is sufficient, and assess whether this influence is recoverable from CoT. Although this influence can appear in the CoT, its detectability varies across models and depends on what is being monitored. Reasoning-trained models are more likely to explicitly refer to the cues, but their longer and fluent CoTs can still appear visually grounded while actually following textual cues, obscuring modality reliance. In contrast, instruction-tuned models refer to the cues less explicitly, but their shorter traces reveal inconsistencies with the visual input. Taken together, these findings indicate that CoT provides only a partial view of how different modalities drive VLM decisions, with important implications for the transparency and safety of multimodal systems.

</details>

Method: 提出IE-as-Cache框架，结合查询驱动的信息抽取与缓存感知的推理机制，借鉴层次化计算机内存设计，动态维护关键中间信息，并抑制无关噪声，实现信息的高效存储与再利用。

Conclusion: 信息抽取不仅可作为信息获取终点，更可作为支持多步推理的可复用认知缓存；本研究为信息抽取在下游任务中的新应用提供了新方向。

Abstract: Information Extraction aims to distill structured, decision-relevant information from unstructured text, serving as a foundation for downstream understanding and reasoning. However, it is traditionally treated merely as a terminal objective: once extracted, the resulting structure is often consumed in isolation rather than maintained and reused during multi-step inference. Moving beyond this, we propose \textit{IE-as-Cache}, a framework that repurposes IE as a cognitive cache to enhance agentic reasoning. Drawing inspiration from hierarchical computer memory, our approach combines query-driven extraction with cache-aware reasoning to dynamically maintain compact intermediate information and filter noise. Experiments on challenging benchmarks across diverse LLMs demonstrate significant improvements in reasoning accuracy, indicating that IE can be effectively repurposed as a reusable cognitive resource and offering a promising direction for future research on downstream uses of IE.

### [125] [XQ-MEval: A Dataset with Cross-lingual Parallel Quality for Benchmarking Translation Metrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14934)
*Jingxuan Liu,Zhi Qu,Jin Tei,Hidetaka Kamigaito,Lemao Liu,Taro Watanabe*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了XQ-MEval，一个半自动构建的多语言翻译评估数据集，用于基准测试翻译指标。通过自动注入MQM定义的错误、母语者筛选和错误合并生成可控质量的伪翻译，形成源-参考-伪翻译三元组，以评估翻译指标的质量。实验揭示了平均评分与人类判断之间的不一致，并首次提供了跨语言评分偏差的实证证据。最后，基于XQ-MEval提出了一种归一化策略，使不同语言的评分分布对齐，提升了多语言评估的公平性和可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多语言翻译系统评估普遍采用跨语言平均评分，但缺乏对翻译指标是否存在跨语言评分偏差的系统研究，主要原因是缺少提供平行质量实例的基准数据集，且专家标注不现实。

Method: 通过自动注入MQM定义的错误到原始译文，由母语者筛选确保可靠性，合并错误生成具有可控质量的伪翻译，再与源句和参考译文组成三元组，构建XQ-MEval数据集，用于评估翻译指标的一致性。

Result: 实验发现平均评分与人类判断存在不一致，首次提供了跨语言评分偏差的实证证据；提出的归一化策略有效对齐不同语言的评分分布，提升了多语言评估的公平性与可靠性。

Conclusion: XQ-MEval为多语言翻译指标评估提供了可靠的基准，揭示了现有方法的局限性，并通过归一化策略显著改善了跨语言评估的公平性与一致性。

Abstract: Automatic evaluation metrics are essential for building multilingual translation systems. The common practice of evaluating these systems is averaging metric scores across languages, yet this is suspicious since metrics may suffer from cross-lingual scoring bias, where translations of equal quality receive different scores across languages. This problem has not been systematically studied because no benchmark exists that provides parallel-quality instances across languages, and expert annotation is not realistic. In this work, we propose XQ-MEval, a semi-automatically built dataset covering nine translation directions, to benchmark translation metrics. Specifically, we inject MQM-defined errors into gold translations automatically, filter them by native speakers for reliability, and merge errors to generate pseudo translations with controllable quality. These pseudo translations are then paired with corresponding sources and references to form triplets used in assessing the qualities of translation metrics. Using XQ-MEval, our experiments on nine representative metrics reveal the inconsistency between averaging and human judgment and provide the first empirical evidence of cross-lingual scoring bias. Finally, we propose a normalization strategy derived from XQ-MEval that aligns score distributions across languages, improving the fairness and reliability of multilingual metric evaluation.

### [128] [IUQ: Interrogative Uncertainty Quantification for Long-Form Large Language Model Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15109)
*Haozhi Fan,Jinhao Duan,Kaidi Xu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为交互式不确定性量化（IUQ）的新框架，旨在解决大语言模型在生成长文本时的不确定性量化难题。该方法通过‘提问-回应’范式，结合样本间一致性与样本内忠实性，有效评估长文本生成中的每个主张层面的不确定性及模型忠实度。实验表明，IUQ在多个模型家族和规模下均优于现有方法，在两个主流长文本生成数据集上表现优异。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在生成长文本时，虽然语义连贯，但常存在事实错误，且缺乏对不确定性与忠实度的有效量化手段，尤其在自由形式生成场景中挑战更大。现有方法多限于短文本或受限输出，难以适用于真实复杂应用。因此亟需一种能衡量长文本生成中每个主张不确定性的新方法。

Method: 提出Interrogative Uncertainty Quantification (IUQ)框架，采用‘提问-回应’范式：先对原始生成内容进行多轮追问以探测其内部一致性；再基于回答的一致性与原始输出的忠实程度，计算每个主张的不确定性得分。利用跨样本一致性与单样本内逻辑自洽性双重指标，实现对长文本生成质量的精细化评估。

Result: 在多个大语言模型（包括不同架构与规模）上进行实验，结果表明IUQ在两个主流长文本生成数据集上显著优于现有基准方法，能够更准确地识别出不准确或高风险的主张，并提供可靠的不确定性评分。

Conclusion: IUQ为长文本生成中的不确定性量化提供了有效解决方案，兼具理论严谨性与实际可操作性，适用于多样化应用场景，推动了可信大语言模型生成的发展。

Abstract: Despite the rapid advancement of Large Language Models (LLMs), uncertainty quantification in LLM generation is a persistent challenge. Although recent approaches have achieved strong performance by restricting LLMs to produce short or constrained answer sets, many real-world applications require long-form and free-form text generation. A key difficulty in this setting is that LLMs often produce responses that are semantically coherent yet factually inaccurate, while the underlying semantics are multifaceted and the linguistic structure is complex. To tackle this challenge, this paper introduces Interrogative Uncertainty Quantification (IUQ), a novel framework that leverages inter-sample consistency and intra-sample faithfulness to quantify the uncertainty in long-form LLM outputs. By utilizing an interrogate-then-respond paradigm, our method provides reliable measures of claim-level uncertainty and the model's faithfulness. Experimental results across diverse model families and model sizes demonstrate the superior performance of IUQ over two widely used long-form generation datasets. The code is available at https://github.com/louisfanhz/IUQ.

</details>


### [129] [DiscoTrace: Representing and Comparing Answering Strategies of Humans and LLMs in Information-Seeking Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15140)
*Neha Srikanth,Jordan Boyd-Graber,Rachel Rudinger*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: DiscoTrace是一种识别回答者在回应信息寻求问题时所使用修辞策略的方法，通过将答案表示为与原始问题解释相关的论述行为序列，并基于修辞结构理论解析。研究发现不同人类社群在答案构建上存在显著差异，而大语言模型（LLM）缺乏这种修辞多样性，且倾向于覆盖更广的解释范围，即使被要求模仿特定社群风格。该研究为开发更具语用意识的、能根据上下文灵活选择策略的LLM问答系统提供了指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型在回答信息寻求问题时缺乏对人类社群中多样修辞策略的理解和模仿能力，导致回答缺乏上下文适应性。因此需要一种方法来识别并分析人类如何以不同修辞方式组织答案，从而改进LLM的回答质量与自然性。

Method: 提出DiscoTrace方法，将答案建模为一系列与问题相关的论述行为，并结合对原问题的解释，基于修辞结构理论进行标注与分析。在九个不同的人类社区数据集上应用该方法，对比人类与LLM的回答模式差异。

Result: 人类社群在构建答案时表现出明显的修辞偏好差异；而尽管经过提示，大语言模型仍缺乏修辞多样性，且倾向于覆盖更多未被人类回答者关注的问题解释，显示出系统性的‘广度偏差’。

Conclusion: 当前的大语言模型在回答策略上缺乏人类的语用多样性，无法有效模仿特定社群的修辞风格。未来应设计更注重上下文与策略多样性的语用型问答系统，以提升回答的自然性与适切性。

Abstract: We introduce DiscoTrace, a method to identify the rhetorical strategies that answerers use when responding to information-seeking questions. DiscoTrace represents answers as a sequence of question-related discourse acts paired with interpretations of the original question, annotated on top of rhetorical structure theory parses. Applying DiscoTrace to answers from nine different human communities reveals that communities have diverse preferences for answer construction. In contrast, LLMs do not exhibit rhetorical diversity in their answers, even when prompted to mimic specific human community answering guidelines. LLMs also systematically opt for breadth, addressing interpretations of questions that human answerers choose not to address. Our findings can guide the development of pragmatic LLM answerers that consider a range of strategies informed by context in QA.

### [130] [Compressing Sequences in the Latent Embedding Space: $K$-Token Merging for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15153)
*Zihao Xu,John Harvill,Ziwei Fan,Yizhou Sun,Hao Ding,Hao Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出K-Token Merging，一种在潜在嵌入空间中进行压缩的框架，通过轻量编码器将每连续K个词元嵌入合并为单一嵌入，以降低长提示处理的计算与内存开销。该方法在保持生成词汇不变的前提下，结合LoRA适配的LLM进行推理，在多个任务上实现了高达75%的输入长度压缩，同时性能损失极小，位于性能与压缩率的帕累托最优前沿。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有提示压缩方法主要在词元空间操作，忽略了潜在嵌入空间中的效率问题，导致无法充分优化长输入下的计算与内存消耗。

Method: 提出K-Token Merging框架，将连续K个词元嵌入通过轻量编码器合并为单个嵌入，压缩后序列由LoRA适配的LLM处理，生成阶段仍使用原始词汇表。

Result: 在结构推理、情感分类和代码编辑任务上，K-Token Merging实现了最高75%的输入长度压缩，性能下降微小，显著优于现有方法，处于性能与压缩比的帕累托最优区域。

Conclusion: K-Token Merging通过在潜在空间进行高效压缩，有效缓解了长提示下大语言模型的计算与内存瓶颈，是一种兼顾性能与压缩效率的先进方案。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) incur significant computational and memory costs when processing long prompts, as full self-attention scales quadratically with input length. Token compression aims to address this challenge by reducing the number of tokens representing inputs. However, existing prompt-compression approaches primarily operate in token space and overlook inefficiencies in the latent embedding space. In this paper, we propose K-Token Merging, a latent-space compression framework that merges each contiguous block of K token embeddings into a single embedding via a lightweight encoder. The compressed sequence is processed by a LoRA-adapted LLM, while generation remains in the original vocabulary. Experiments on structural reasoning (Textualized Tree), sentiment classification (Amazon Reviews), and code editing (CommitPackFT) show that K-Token Merging lies on the Pareto frontier of performance vs. compression, achieving up to 75% input length reduction with minimal performance degradation.

*Raunak Agarwal,Markus Wenzel,Simon Baur,Jonas Zimmer,George Harvey,Jackie Ma*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出MADE，一个持续更新的多标签文本分类基准，用于医疗设备不良事件报告，以解决数据污染和标签不平衡问题。评估了多种模型和不确定性量化方法，发现小规模判别性微调解码器在准确率和不确定性量化上表现最佳，生成式微调提供最可靠的不确定性估计，而大型推理模型虽提升罕见标签性能但不确定性表现差，自言自语置信度不可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多标签文本分类基准存在数据污染和饱和问题，难以区分模型的真实推理能力与记忆现象；医疗领域需要可靠且可解释的不确定性量化来支持人类监督。

Method: 构建MADE基准，基于医学设备不良事件报告，采用时间划分保证可重复性；评估20多个编码器-解码器模型在微调与少样本设置下的表现；系统比较熵/一致性为基础及自言自语的不确定性量化方法。

Result: 小规模判别性微调解码器在头尾标签准确率和UQ上表现优异；生成式微调提供最可靠的UQ；大模型提升稀有标签性能但UQ弱；自言自语置信度不能有效反映真实不确定性。

Conclusion: MADE是一个可持续、防污染的多标签文本分类基准，能有效评估模型在医疗场景中的预测性能与不确定性量化能力，为高风险领域的可信机器学习提供了重要工具。

Abstract: Machine learning in high-stakes domains such as healthcare requires not only strong predictive performance but also reliable uncertainty quantification (UQ) to support human oversight. Multi-label text classification (MLTC) is a central task in this domain, yet remains challenging due to label imbalances, dependencies, and combinatorial complexity. Existing MLTC benchmarks are increasingly saturated and may be affected by training data contamination, making it difficult to distinguish genuine reasoning capabilities from memorization. We introduce MADE, a living MLTC benchmark derived from {m}edical device {ad}verse {e}vent reports and continuously updated with newly published reports to prevent contamination. MADE features a long-tailed distribution of hierarchical labels and enables reproducible evaluation with strict temporal splits. We establish baselines across more than 20 encoder- and decoder-only models under fine-tuning and few-shot settings (instruction-tuned/reasoning variants, local/API-accessible). We systematically assess entropy-/consistency-based and self-verbalized UQ methods. Results show clear trade-offs: smaller discriminatively fine-tuned decoders achieve the strongest head-to-tail accuracy while maintaining competitive UQ; generative fine-tuning delivers the most reliable UQ; large reasoning models improve performance on rare labels yet exhibit surprisingly weak UQ; and self-verbalized confidence is not a reliable proxy for uncertainty. Our work is publicly available at https://hhi.fraunhofer.de/aml-demonstrator/made-benchmark.

</details>


### [133] [From Tokens to Steps: Verification-Aware Speculative Decoding for Efficient Multi-Step Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15244)
*Kiran Purohit,Ramasuri Narayanam,Soumyabrata Pal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SpecGuard提出一种仅使用模型内部信号的验证感知推测解码框架，通过在每一步采样多个草稿候选并选择最一致的步骤，利用两个轻量级模型内信号（注意力基定位得分和基于对数概率的置信度得分）进行步骤级验证，从而选择性分配计算资源。实验表明，该方法在多个推理基准上将准确率提升3.6%，同时降低约11%的延迟，优于传统推测解码和基于奖励模型的推测解码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推测解码方法依赖外部奖励模型进行错误修正，带来额外延迟、计算开销且泛化能力受限。为解决此问题，需设计一种无需外部信号、仅依赖模型内部信息的高效验证机制。

Method: SpecGuard在每一步采样多个草稿候选，通过两个轻量级模型内信号——注意力基接地分数（衡量输入与已接受步骤的归属度）和对数概率分数（捕捉词元置信度）——联合判断是否接受当前步骤或重新计算。

Result: 在多个推理基准测试中，SpecGuard相比标准推测解码提升3.6%准确率，同时减少约11%的延迟，表现优于传统推测解码及基于奖励模型的方法。

Conclusion: SpecGuard通过利用模型内部信号实现高效的步骤级验证，在不引入外部依赖的前提下显著提升了推测解码的准确性与效率，为大语言模型推理优化提供了一种高效、通用的新方案。

Abstract: Speculative decoding (SD) accelerates large language model inference by allowing a lightweight draft model to propose outputs that a stronger target model verifies. However, its token-centric nature allows erroneous steps to propagate. Prior approaches mitigate this using external reward models, but incur additional latency, computational overhead, and limit generalizability. We propose SpecGuard, a verification-aware speculative decoding framework that performs step-level verification using only model-internal signals. At each step, SpecGuard samples multiple draft candidates and selects the most consistent step, which is then validated using an ensemble of two lightweight model-internal signals: (i) an attention-based grounding score that measures attribution to the input and previously accepted steps, and (ii) a log-probability-based score that captures token-level confidence. These signals jointly determine whether a step is accepted or recomputed using the target, allocating compute selectively. Experiments across a range of reasoning benchmarks show that SpecGuard improves accuracy by 3.6% while reducing latency by ~11%, outperforming both SD and reward-guided SD.

</details>

### [134] [The Devil Is in Gradient Entanglement: Energy-Aware Gradient Coordinator for Robust Generalized Category Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14176)
*Haiyang Zheng,Nan Pu,Yaqi Cai,Teng Long,Wenjing Li,Nicu Sebe,Zhun Zhong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出EAGC解决GCD中的梯度纠缠问题，通过AGA和EEP组件分别实现梯度方向对齐与能量感知投影，显著提升模型性能并达到新SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GCD方法因监督与无监督目标优化干扰导致梯度纠缠，影响已知类判别性和新类别可分性，亟需更有效的梯度协调机制。

Method: 提出EAGC模块，包含锚定梯度对齐（AGA）和能量感知弹性投影（EEP），分别控制已知类样本梯度方向并自适应调节未标记样本梯度投影以减少子空间重叠。

Result: EAGC在多个基准上持续提升现有方法性能，取得新的最佳结果，代码已开源。

Conclusion: EAGC有效缓解梯度纠缠问题，增强了已知与未知类别的分离能力，为GCD提供了高效的梯度协调新范式。

Abstract: Generalized Category Discovery (GCD) leverages labeled data to categorize unlabeled samples from known or unknown classes. Most previous methods jointly optimize supervised and unsupervised objectives and achieve promising results. However, inherent optimization interference still limits their ability to improve further. Through quantitative analysis, we identify a key issue, i.e., gradient entanglement, which 1) distorts supervised gradients and weakens discrimination among known classes, and 2) induces representation-subspace overlap between known and novel classes, reducing the separability of novel categories. To address this issue, we propose the Energy-Aware Gradient Coordinator (EAGC), a plug-and-play gradient-level module that explicitly regulates the optimization process. EAGC comprises two components: Anchor-based Gradient Alignment (AGA) and Energy-aware Elastic Projection (EEP). AGA introduces a reference model to anchor the gradient directions of labeled samples, preserving the discriminative structure of known classes against the interference of unlabeled gradients. EEP softly projects unlabeled gradients onto the complement of the known-class subspace and derives an energy-based coefficient to adaptively scale the projection for each unlabeled sample according to its degree of alignment with the known subspace, thereby reducing subspace overlap without suppressing unlabeled samples that likely belong to known classes. Experiments show that EAGC consistently boosts existing methods and establishes new state-of-the-art results. Code is available at https://haiyangzheng.github.io/EAGC.

</details>


### [135] [Towards Verified and Targeted Explanations through Formal Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14209)
*Hanchen David Wang,Diego Manzanas Lopez,Preston K. Robinette,Ipek Oguz,Taylor T. Johnson,Meiyi Ma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ViTaX 是一种新型的可解释人工智能（XAI）框架，旨在为安全关键系统提供具有数学保证的靶向半事实解释。它通过识别对特定类别转换最敏感的最小特征子集，并利用形式化可达性分析证明这些特征在扰动范围内不会导致模型分类为指定目标类，从而实现对模型对抗用户指定风险的稳健性验证。该方法首次实现了针对特定威胁场景的可验证解释，在多个基准数据集上表现出超过30%的解释保真度提升，同时保持极低的解释复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的XAI方法要么缺乏数学保证（如LIME、Integrated Gradients），要么不具针对性（如传统形式化方法），无法有效应对安全关键系统中不同误判带来的非均衡风险。例如，将“停车”标志误认为“60公里/小时”标志比误认为“禁止超车”标志更具危险性。因此需要一种既能提供可解释性又能确保对关键风险进行形式化验证的方法。

Method: ViTaX提出了一种名为‘靶向epsilon鲁棒性’的形式化定义，用于衡量在扰动下某个特征子集是否仍能避免被分类到用户指定的目标类。其核心流程包括：(1) 识别影响从真实类别y到目标类别t转换的最小敏感特征子集；(2) 使用形式化可达性分析，严格证明在不超过ε的扰动范围内，该特征子集不会使模型输出变为目标类。

Result: 在MNIST、GTSRB、EMNIST和TaxiNet等多个数据集上的实验表明，ViTaX相比现有方法在解释保真度上提升超过30%，且解释的特征数量极少，说明其在保持高精度的同时具备良好的简洁性与实用性。

Conclusion: ViTaX是首个能够为用户指定的关键替代类别提供形式化保障的可解释性框架，显著提升了深度学习模型在安全关键应用中的可信度与可解释性，为未来面向高风险场景的AI系统设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: As deep neural networks are deployed in safety-critical domains such as autonomous driving and medical diagnosis, stakeholders need explanations that are interpretable but also trustworthy with formal guarantees. Existing XAI methods fall short: heuristic attribution techniques (e.g., LIME, Integrated Gradients) highlight influential features but offer no mathematical guarantees about decision boundaries, while formal methods verify robustness yet remain untargeted, analyzing the nearest boundary regardless of whether it represents a critical risk. In safety-critical systems, not all misclassifications carry equal consequences; confusing a "Stop" sign for a "60 kph" sign is far more dangerous than confusing it with a "No Passing" sign. We introduce ViTaX (Verified and Targeted Explanations), a formal XAI framework that generates targeted semifactual explanations with mathematical guarantees. For a given input (class y) and a user-specified critical alternative (class t), ViTaX: (1) identifies the minimal feature subset most sensitive to the y->t transition, and (2) applies formal reachability analysis to guarantee that perturbing these features by epsilon cannot flip the classification to t. We formalize this through Targeted epsilon-Robustness, certifying whether a feature subset remains robust under perturbation toward a specific target class. ViTaX is the first method to provide formally guaranteed explanations of a model's resilience against user-identified alternatives. Evaluations on MNIST, GTSRB, EMNIST, and TaxiNet demonstrate over 30% fidelity improvement with minimal explanation cardinality.

</details>


### [136] [Shapley Value-Guided Adaptive Ensemble Learning for Explainable Financial Fraud Detection with U.S. Regulatory Compliance Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14231)
*Mohammad Nasir Uddin,Md Munna Aziz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究针对金融犯罪检测中AI模型缺乏透明性的问题，评估了多种模型的解释质量，并提出SHAP-Guided Adaptive Ensemble（SGAE）模型以提升可解释性和性能。在IEEE-CIS数据集上，GNN-GraphSAGE表现最佳，AUC-ROC达0.9248，F1为0.6013；SGAE在跨验证中达到0.9245 AUC-ROC，且所有结果均符合OCC、SR 11-7和BSA-AML监管要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前金融欺诈检测中的AI模型多为黑箱，难以满足监管机构对透明性和可审计性的要求，如OCC Bulletin 2011-12和Federal Reserve SR 11-7。因此亟需兼具高性能与高可解释性的模型解决方案。

Method: 采用多种解释方法（如TreeExplainer、DeepExplainer）评估模型解释质量，包括忠实性（k=5,10,15时的充分性与完备性）和稳定性（30次自助采样下的Kendall's W）。提出SHAP-Guided Adaptive Ensemble（SGAE），根据SHAP值一致性动态调整集成权重。同时在完整数据集上对比LSTM、Transformer和GNN-GraphSAGE三种架构的性能。

Result: XGBoost+TreeExplainer在稳定性上表现优异（W=0.9912），而LSTM+DeepExplainer表现差（W=0.4962）。SGAE在测试集上取得0.8837的AUC-ROC，交叉验证达0.9245。GNN-GraphSAGE在全量数据上实现AUC-ROC 0.9248和F1=0.6013。所有结果均映射至相关监管合规要求。

Conclusion: 本研究通过系统评估解释质量并引入SGAE模型，成功构建了一个既高效又符合监管要求的金融欺诈检测框架，为实际部署提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Financial crime costs U.S. institutions over $32 billion each year. Although AI tools for fraud detection have become more advanced, their use in real-world systems still faces a major obstacle: many of these models operate as black boxes that cannot provide the transparent, auditable explanations required by regulations such as OCC Bulletin 2011-12 and Federal Reserve SR 11-7. This study makes three main contributions. First, it offers a thorough evaluation of explanation quality across faithfulness (sufficiency and comprehensiveness at k=5, 10, and 15) and stability (Kendall's W across 30 bootstrap samples). XGBoost paired with TreeExplainer achieves near-perfect stability (W=0.9912), while LSTM with DeepExplainer shows weak results (W=0.4962). Second, the paper introduces the SHAP-Guided Adaptive Ensemble (SGAE), which dynamically adjusts per-transaction ensemble weights based on SHAP attribution agreement, achieving the highest AUC-ROC among all tested models (0.8837 held-out; 0.9245 cross-validation). Third, a complete three-architecture evaluation of LSTM, Transformer, and GNN-GraphSAGE on the full 590,540-transaction IEEE-CIS dataset is provided, with GNN-GraphSAGE achieving AUC-ROC 0.9248 and F1=0.6013. All results are mapped directly to OCC, SR 11-7, and BSA-AML regulatory compliance requirements.

</details>


### [137] [Graph-Based Fraud Detection with Dual-Path Graph Filtering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14235)
*Wei He,Wensheng Gan,Philip S. Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于双路径图滤波的图欺诈检测模型（DPF-GFD），通过结合原始图与相似性图的双重过滤机制，有效应对欺诈图中的关系伪装、高异质性和类别不平衡问题。该方法利用贝塔小波算子捕捉结构模式，并通过改进的低通滤波器在相似性图上进行特征平滑，再通过监督表示学习融合两种图的嵌入表示，最终由集成树模型评估节点欺诈风险。实验在四个真实金融欺诈数据集上验证了其优越性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 欺诈图具有关系伪装、高异质性和类别不平衡等特性，导致现有GNN模型在欺诈检测任务中表现不佳，亟需更有效的图建模方法来提升检测性能。

Method: 提出DPF-GFD模型，首先使用贝塔小波算子对原始图进行结构模式提取；其次构建基于距离的节点表示相似性图，并应用改进的低通滤波器进行平滑；最后通过监督学习融合原始图与相似性图的嵌入表示，输入集成树模型进行欺诈风险评估。

Result: 在四个真实世界金融欺诈数据集上的实验表明，DPF-GFD显著优于现有基线方法，在欺诈检测准确率和稳定性方面均有明显提升。

Conclusion: DPF-GFD通过频率互补的双路径图滤波设计，有效解耦了结构异常建模与特征相似性建模，提升了在高度异质和不平衡欺诈图中的节点表示能力，为图欺诈检测提供了新范式。

Abstract: Fraud detection on graph data can be viewed as a demanding task that requires distinguishing between different types of nodes. Because graph neural networks (GNNs) are naturally suited for processing information encoded in graph form through their message-passing operations, methods based on GNN models have increasingly attracted attention in the fraud detection domain. However, fraud graphs inherently exhibit relation camouflage, high heterophily, and class imbalance, causing most GNNs to underperform in fraud detection tasks. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a Graph-Based Fraud Detection Model with Dual-Path Graph Filtering (DPF-GFD). DPF-GFD first applies a beta wavelet-based operator to the original graph to capture key structural patterns. It then constructs a similarity graph from distance-based node representations and applies an improved low-pass filter. The embeddings from the original and similarity graphs are fused through supervised representation learning to obtain node features, which are finally used by an ensemble tree model to assess the fraud risk of unlabeled nodes. Unlike existing single-graph smoothing approaches, DPF-GFD introduces a frequency-complementary dual-path filtering paradigm tailored for fraud detection, explicitly decoupling structural anomaly modeling and feature similarity modeling. This design enables more discriminative and stable node representations in highly heterophilous and imbalanced fraud graphs. Comprehensive experiments on four real-world financial fraud detection datasets demonstrate the effectiveness of our proposed method.

</details>


### [138] [TOPCELL: Topology Optimization of Standard Cell via LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14237)
*Zhan Song,Yu-Tung Liu,Chen Chen,Guoheng Sun,Jiaqi Yin,Chia-tung Ho,Ang Li,Haoxing Ren,Cunxi Yu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将拓扑优化重构为生成任务，采用大语言模型（LLM）进行建模，并结合组相对策略优化（GRPO）对齐电路逻辑与物理布局约束，实现高效且符合实际需求的拓扑生成。

Result: 在2nm工艺节点实验中，TOPCELL在可布线拓扑发现能力上显著超越基础模型；在7nm库生成任务中，实现零样本泛化，布局质量接近穷举求解器，同时获得85.91倍的速度提升。

Conclusion: TOPCELL成功将大语言模型应用于晶体管拓扑优化，克服了传统方法的可扩展性瓶颈，在保证布局质量的同时极大提升了设计效率，为先进制程下的标准单元自动化设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: Transistor topology optimization is a critical step in standard cell design, directly dictating diffusion sharing efficiency and downstream routability. However, identifying optimal topologies remains a persistent bottleneck, as conventional exhaustive search methods become computationally intractable with increasing circuit complexity in advanced nodes. This paper introduces TOPCELL, a novel and scalable framework that reformulates high-dimensional topology exploration as a generative task using Large Language Models (LLMs). We employ Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to fine-tune the model, aligning its topology optimization strategy with logical (circuit) and spatial (layout) constraints. Experimental results within an industrial flow targeting an advanced 2nm technology node demonstrate that TOPCELL significantly outperforms foundation models in discovering routable, physically-aware topologies. When integrated into a state-of-the-art (SOTA) automation flow for a 7nm library generation task, TOPCELL exhibits robust zero-shot generalization and matches the layout quality of exhaustive solvers while achieving an 85.91x speedup.

### [139] [Awakening Dormant Experts:Counterfactual Routing to Mitigate MoE Hallucinations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14246)
*Wentao Hu,Yanbo Zhai,Xiaohui Hu,Mingkuan Zhao,Shanhong yu,Xue Liu,Kaidong Yu,Shuangyong Song,Xuelong Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为Counterfactual Routing (CoR)的无训练推理框架，旨在解决稀疏混合专家（MoE）模型在处理长尾知识时易产生幻觉的问题。该方法通过层间扰动分析与反事实专家影响（CEI）度量，动态调整计算资源分配，唤醒原本处于‘休眠’状态的关键专家，提升模型对罕见事实的捕捉能力。实验表明，CoR在不增加推理开销的前提下，平均提升事实准确性3.1%，优于传统静态扩展策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有稀疏混合专家（MoE）模型因采用静态Top-k路由机制，倾向于优先选择高频模式，导致掌握关键长尾知识的专家被忽视，无法有效激活，从而引发幻觉问题。

Method: 提出Counterfactual Routing (CoR)，利用层级扰动分析和反事实专家影响（CEI）度量，在推理阶段动态调整专家激活路径，实现从语法主导层向知识密集型层的资源转移，保持总激活数不变，通过虚拟消融方式唤醒关键专家。

Result: 在TruthfulQA、FACTOR和TriviaQA等多个数据集上，CoR平均提升事实准确性3.1%，且无需额外推理成本，构建了优于静态扩展策略的更优帕累托前沿。

Conclusion: CoR是一种高效、无需训练的推理优化框架，能有效缓解MoE模型在长尾知识上的脆弱性，显著提升事实准确性，为大规模语言模型的可靠性和可解释性提供了新思路。

Abstract: Sparse Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models have achieved remarkable scalability, yet they remain vulnerable to hallucinations, particularly when processing long-tail knowledge. We identify that this fragility stems from static Top-$k$ routing: routers tend to favor high-frequency patterns over rare factual associations. Consequently, ``specialist experts'' possessing critical long-tail knowledge are often assigned low gating scores and remain ``dormant'' -- under-prioritized for specific tokens despite their proven causal importance on other inputs. To address this, we propose Counterfactual Routing (CoR), a training-free inference framework designed to awaken these dormant experts. CoR integrates layer-wise perturbation analysis with the Counterfactual Expert Impact (CEI) metric to dynamically shift computational resources from syntax-dominant to knowledge-intensive layers while maintaining a constant total activation count, effectively retrieving causally decisive experts via virtual ablation. Extensive experiments on TruthfulQA, FACTOR, and TriviaQA demonstrate that CoR improves factual accuracy by 3.1\% on average without increasing the inference budget, establishing a superior Pareto frontier compared to static scaling strategies.

</details>


### [140] [Metric-Aware Principal Component Analysis (MAPCA):A Unified Framework for Scale-Invariant Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14249)
*Michael Leznik*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种统一的尺度不变表示学习框架——度量感知主成分分析（MAPCA），通过广义特征值问题最大化 Tr(W^T Sigma W) 并满足 W^T M W = I，其中 M 为对称正定度量矩阵。通过选择不同的 M，可控制表示几何结构。特别地，引入 beta-族度量 M(beta) = Sigma^beta（beta ∈ [0,1]），实现了从标准PCA（beta=0）到输出白化（beta=1）的连续谱偏差控制，并使条件数单调下降至各向同性。对角度量 M = diag(Sigma) 恢复了不变主成分分析（IPCA），属于该框架的特例。研究证明，尺度不变性仅在度量按 M_tilde = CMC 变换时成立，这仅精确满足于 IPCA，而不适用于中间 beta 值的通用 beta-族。此外，MAPCA 提供了一个几何语言，统一了多种自监督学习目标：Barlow Twins 和 ZCA 白化对应 beta=1；VICReg 的方差项对应对角度量；而 W-MSE 实际对应 M = Sigma^{-1}（beta=-1），位于谱压缩范围之外且与 Barlow Twins 方向相反，这一关键区别在损失函数层面无法察觉，必须借助 MAPCA 框架才能明确揭示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有主成分分析方法在尺度不变性和表示几何控制方面存在局限，尤其难以统一解释不同自监督学习目标背后的几何本质。本文旨在建立一个统一的、可调控的框架，以揭示和连接传统统计方法与现代自监督学习方法之间的深层联系，并实现对表示学习中尺度不变性的精确建模与控制。

Method: 提出基于广义特征值问题 max Tr(W^T Sigma W) subject to W^T M W = I 的度量感知主成分分析（MAPCA）框架。引入参数化度量矩阵 M(beta) = Sigma^beta（beta ∈ [0,1]），实现连续谱偏差控制；分析对角度量情形下的 IPCA 关系；严格推导尺度不变性条件；将多种自监督学习目标（如 Barlow Twins、VICReg、W-MSE）映射至该框架中的特定度量形式，揭示其几何本质差异。

Result: MAPCA 框架成功统一了标准 PCA、输出白化、不变 PCA 及多种自监督学习目标；揭示了 W-MSE 实际对应于 M = Sigma^{-1}（beta=-1），与常规白化方向相反，且不在谱压缩范围内；证明了尺度不变性仅在 IPCA 下精确成立，而 beta-族在中间值不满足；展示了该框架在理解表示学习几何结构方面的强大统一能力。

Conclusion: MAPCA 为尺度不变表示学习提供了一个统一、可解释且具有几何意义的框架，不仅深化了对传统主成分分析的理解，也揭示了自监督学习方法之间隐藏的几何差异。该框架强调了度量选择在表示学习中的核心作用，并为未来设计更具可控性和理论保障的表示学习方法提供了新视角。

Abstract: We introduce Metric-Aware Principal Component Analysis (MAPCA), a unified framework for scale-invariant representation learning based on the generalised eigenproblem max Tr(W^T Sigma W) subject to W^T M W = I, where M is a symmetric positive definite metric matrix. The choice of M determines the representation geometry. The canonical beta-family M(beta) = Sigma^beta, beta in [0,1], provides continuous spectral bias control between standard PCA (beta=0) and output whitening (beta=1), with condition number kappa(beta) = (lambda_1/lambda_p)^(1-beta) decreasing monotonically to isotropy. The diagonal metric M = D = diag(Sigma) recovers Invariant PCA (IPCA), a method rooted in Frisch (1928) diagonal regression, as a distinct member of the broader framework. We prove that scale invariance holds if and only if the metric transforms as M_tilde = CMC under rescaling C, a condition satisfied exactly by IPCA but not by the general beta-family at intermediate values.
  Beyond its classical interpretation, MAPCA provides a geometric language that unifies several self-supervised learning objectives. Barlow Twins and ZCA whitening correspond to beta=1 (output whitening); VICReg's variance term corresponds to the diagonal metric. A key finding is that W-MSE, despite being described as a whitening-based method, corresponds to M = Sigma^{-1} (beta = -1), outside the spectral compression range entirely and in the opposite spectral direction to Barlow Twins. This distinction between input and output whitening is invisible at the level of loss functions and becomes precise only within the MAPCA framework.

</details>


### [141] [GUI-Perturbed: Domain Randomization Reveals Systematic Brittleness in GUI Grounding Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14262)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: GUI-Perturbed is a controlled perturbation framework that independently varies visual elements and instructions to measure model robustness across multiple axes: spatial reasoning, visual robustness, and reasoning calibration.

Result: Relational instructions cause significant accuracy drops across all tested models; 70% zoom leads to statistically significant degradation; rank-8 LoRA fine-tuning with augmented data harms performance instead of improving it.

Abstract: GUI grounding models report over 85% accuracy on standard benchmarks, yet drop 27-56 percentage points when instructions require spatial reasoning rather than direct element naming. Current benchmarks miss this because they evaluate each screenshot once with a single fixed instruction. We introduce GUI-Perturbed, a controlled perturbation framework that independently varies visual scenes and instructions to measure grounding robustness. Evaluating three 7B models from the same architecture lineage, we find that relational instructions cause systematic accuracy collapse across all models, a 70% browser zoom produces statistically significant degradation, and rank-8 LoRA fine-tuning with augmented data degrades performance rather than improving it. By perturbing along independent axes, GUI-Perturbed isolates which specific capability axes are affected-spatial reasoning, visual robustness, reasoning calibration-providing diagnostic signal that aggregate benchmarks cannot. We release the dataset, augmentation pipeline, and a fine-tuned model.
